(8th dispatch) Foreign Telegrams

Brüning

Ordered to Form New Cabinet

The German People No Longer Have Freedom

Reuters, Berlin, 7th: Brüning, at the request of President Hindenburg, is currently organizing a list of new cabinet members, which may be completed tomorrow, so that the new government can be realized within 24 hours after the resignation of the old government. It is generally expected that Brüning will also serve as Foreign Minister himself to show that Germany will not change its foreign policy. However, there are many doubts about the lifespan of the cabinet. If the National People's Party and the United National Rights Party vote against the new government, its lifespan will come to an end. In that case, Brüning must obtain the consent of President Hindenburg to openly declare a dictatorship to govern the country without the need for parliament. Otherwise, Hitler's followers will have the opportunity to take charge of state affairs. Ordinary Germans may not vehemently oppose a dictatorship, because the recent emergency orders have already been equivalent to a dictatorship. The latest order issued today still reduces civil rights, so it can be said that there is no longer freedom of the people in Germany today.

National News Agency, Berlin, 7th: Dr. Brüning is currently doing his best to handle government affairs as usual. The new cabinet will be formed at the earliest tomorrow night, because not all of the people Brüning wants to recruit into the cabinet are in Nanjing. The people Brüning is looking for, such as Ambassador to the UK Neu and former Defense Minister Gessler, are still on their way. The situation will only be clear after they arrive in Nanjing tomorrow morning and meet with Brüning. Neu is the most popular candidate for Foreign Minister. If he is unwilling to accept the position, Brüning may temporarily serve as Foreign Minister himself. Gessler is expected to be the Minister of Interior. Schmitz is designated to be the Minister of Communications. The three, in addition to being conservative, have no party affiliation and will join the cabinet as experts. The other two experts are the current permanent Vice-Minister of Justice Gurl, who is expected to be promoted to Minister, and former Prussian Cabinet Minister of Agriculture and Forestry Hua Hede, who will be the Minister of Economy. It is reported that the two have agreed to join Brüning's new cabinet. The old cabinet members who will continue to serve are Minister of Agriculture and Forestry Heier, Minister of Finance Dietrel, Minister of Defense Groener, and Minister of Posts Schätzel. Brüning hopes that the reorganized cabinet can obtain the support of a majority in parliament, but because the Social Democratic Party does not unanimously support Brüning, success or failure is still uncertain. Political circles denied last night that the emergency order had dictatorial characteristics, but all circles expressed dissatisfaction with it.

British Prime Minister Issues Declaration

Starts Election Campaign

Reuters, London, 7th: British Prime Minister MacDonald has issued a declaration, starting his election campaign. The declaration outlines the organization and work of the National Government, and continues to say that danger remains, and the most important methods should be adopted both internally and externally to balance the budget and restore credit. He also said that the National Government must participate in international conferences to discuss the world's economic and financial situation, and use its power to remove commercial and financial obstacles. These obstacles are the uneconomical distribution of war debts and reparations, and the stagnation of debts. It is difficult to determine the strategies to deal with the situation. The government must consider its own proposals based on the circumstances, such as tax cuts, import reductions, commercial agreements, and mutual economic arrangements for overseas autonomous territories. The remedies required by the situation cannot be implemented by parties that only engage in partisan disputes, but must be implemented through the voluntary cooperation of all parties. Therefore, elections cannot be avoided. Please support the National Government so that the world can see the determination of the British people to support any plan that can restore credit with one heart and one mind in the face of national difficulties. Conservative Party Bauer and Liberal Party Samuel will both issue declarations tomorrow calling on the British people to support the National Government. About 50 members of the Parliamentary Labour Party have now formed the National Labour Party to support MacDonald.

British Parliament Closed Yesterday

Reuters, London, 7th: After the passage of the Prohibition of Food Hoarding Bill, Parliament was closed today. The British Emperor's closing speech mentioned the financial panic and the Indian Round Table Conference. The British Emperor then opened a privy council and signed an order to dissolve Parliament.

Meeting of British and French Foreign Ministers

Issues of Disarmament and World Crisis

National News Agency, Paris, 7th: No communiqué was issued on the talks between British Foreign Secretary Reading and French Foreign Minister Briand, but it is understood that they proceeded smoothly. Reading speaks French very fluently, so there was no interpreter present during the talks between the British and French Foreign Ministers. The content of the talks has not been revealed, but it is understood that the two Foreign Ministers discussed issues of disarmament and the world crisis. The talks were mostly in the nature of reports, so there were no concrete results. Regarding the issue of disarmament, it is rumored that Reading is currently making a final effort to reconcile France and Italy.

Reuters, Paris, 7th: According to political circles, British Foreign Secretary Reading said that the British government intends to stabilize the pound as soon as possible after the general election. It is rumored that the French government has agreed to do its best to help the British government achieve this goal. Today, after British Foreign Secretary Reading, French Prime Minister Laval, Foreign Minister Briand, Finance Minister Flandin, and Commerce Minister Rollin held talks, a communiqué stated that the leaders of the two countries sincerely exchanged opinions on various matters related to the overall situation. Talks will continue at 11:00 AM on Thursday.

US Bankers Association Agrees

Organizing a Lending Institution

Reuters, New York, 7th. President Hoover's proposal to organize a lending institution has had a positive impact in banking circles. Members of the New York Clearing House have agreed to contribute $150 million towards the capital of a $500 million lending institution. Leading bankers say the plan is expected to be finalized by the end of this week. The American Bankers Association, meeting in Atlantic City, has endorsed the proposal to organize a lending institution. President Hoover's proposed lending institution at the White House yesterday aims to expand the facilities provided by the Farm Board and the discount provisions of the Federal Reserve Act, in order to reverse the current global economic panic. President Hoover, after consulting with Treasury officials, Federal Reserve governors, and representatives from both houses of Congress, issued a statement saying that major banks are now initiating the organization of a $500 million lending institution, which, if necessary, can be the same as the wartime financial institutions of the past, with the government providing sufficient funding to meet its legitimate needs. This morning, another important meeting was held at the White House in Washington to discuss the proposal to organize a central mortgage and discount bank.

Reuters, Tokyo, 8th. The Governor of the Bank of Japan, Tsuchifang, criticized President Hoover's proposal to improve the U.S. economic situation, saying that he does not believe the current state of decline can be easily cured.

Resolution of the Russian-German Dispute

National News Agency, Berlin, 7th. The Russian-German Arbitration Committee held its final meeting today and signed an agreement, thus resolving all outstanding issues between Russia and Germany. The committee was established after the restoration of the Russian-German Treaty last July. Among the outstanding issues resolved today, the status of representatives such as German commercial experts in Russia and the responsibilities of contracts concluded by the Russian Commercial Commission in Berlin were clearly defined.

Mr. Bittman's Speech on the Silver Question

National News Agency, Washington, 7th. Senator Bittman gave a speech on the radio tonight, broadcast nationwide, claiming that if an international silver conference is convened and agrees to stop dumping silver, the price of silver will immediately double, returning to 60 cents per ounce. At that time, it would greatly increase foreign trade between China and Mexico. He also said that if a silver conference is not convened and there is no immediate remedy for the price of silver, the danger of Britain's isolation in world trade will certainly be realized. It is reported that Bittman, along with Bola and Smote, are leaders of the silver faction in the Senate. Bittman is a Democrat, while Bola and Shi are Republicans. Reuters, Washington, 8th. Representatives attending the Pacific Business Conference met today and advocated convening an international conference to study the restoration of silver prices.

The Indian Round Table Conference Remains Deadlocked

Reuters, London, 7th. The work of the Indian Round Table Conference has stalled because Hindus, Muslims, and other minorities have been unable to agree on the number of seats in the Indian parliament. Subsequently, twenty Indian members of the Round Table Conference formed a committee, chaired by Gandhi, to mediate. After a week, at the final meeting tonight, Gandhi admitted that all efforts had been unsuccessful.

Important News

Manchurian Incident

First Verbal Battle Between China and Japan

At the Council of the League of Nations on the Afternoon of the 19th

The Japanese Representative, Aware of Their Wrongdoing, Made Excuses and Cover-Ups

Our Side Only Made a Simple Statement Due to Not Receiving Detailed Reports

Special Dispatch from Geneva: Japan took advantage of our country's unpreparedness, attacked Manchuria at night, invaded our country's sovereignty, and violated international conventions. Japan should bear full responsibility. However, the Japanese are cunning by nature and do not hesitate to fabricate facts and spread all kinds of rumors internationally to cover up the eyes and ears of the world, saying that this war was a legitimate defense on the part of Japan because the Chinese army demolished the South Manchurian Railway. When the Japanese army came forward to stop them, the Chinese soldiers refused to listen and instead opened fire. The Japanese soldiers had no choice but to return fire. Therefore, the Japanese army's attack on China was out of self-defense. Those familiar with the situation in our country will naturally know the inside story of the Japanese wording, but those who are not familiar with the situation will find it difficult to understand the truth. Therefore, people from all countries hope that both China and Japan will make factual statements in order to clarify the truth. On the afternoon of the 19th of this month, the Council of the League of Nations met. Our country's representative took office as a member of the Executive Committee and discussed major international issues at the same time. Everyone believed that the Chinese and Japanese representatives would inevitably engage in a fierce confrontation, each defending their own country, in order to awaken the ears and eyes of the world. Therefore, the audience attending the meeting that day was packed. The meeting began at 5:00 p.m. The Japanese representative (Ambassador to Paris) was the first to stand up and speak. His speech was as follows: "Mr. Chairman, according to newspaper reports, an accident occurred near Shenyang last night. I would very much like to report the first news I received to the Council, and I am grateful for your permission. Unfortunately, this news is not very detailed. What I can tell you is that Chinese and Japanese troops have clashed in Shenyang and near the South Manchurian Railway. Since hearing this news, the Japanese government has taken all possible measures to prevent this local incident from escalating. I have now asked my government for detailed information. I am confident that it will do its utmost to calm the matter."

The Japanese representative knew yesterday that this act of his country trampled on international conventions and destroyed world peace, which was intolerable to righteousness. Therefore, he tried his best to minimize the problem and make this cunning cover-up. From these few words, his embarrassment can be seen. Our country is justified, and many opinions from all parties also support us. Moreover, our country was recently elected as a member of the Executive Committee, and we can take advantage of the opportunity to inform the world of the source of Japan's invasion of our country in the form of a report. However, at that time, our country's representative, Shi Zhaoji, had not yet received a detailed report from the country, and the truth was not clear. Therefore, his first statement was very cautious and only made the following statement: "Mr. Chairman, since the news of the accident in Manzhouli came (that is, what the Japanese representative just stated), I have been deeply disturbed after hearing it. According to the report I have received so far, China does not seem to have taken any action that would cause this accident. If I receive official news about this unfortunate incident in the future, I will report it to the Council." After our country's representative spoke, the acting chairman of the Council, Lai Ru Leroux (Spanish Foreign Minister), stood up and said, "We have heard the statements of the Chinese and Japanese representatives. The Council is very pleased to hear that the Japanese government will take necessary measures to ease this situation. It goes without saying that I and all the members present sincerely hope that this issue can be resolved as soon as possible." After the chairman finished speaking, other issues were discussed. Japan deliberately invaded China, disregarded the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and despised the provisions of Article 12 of the Covenant of the League of Nations. However, the League of Nations, which claims to maintain world peace, only concluded it with the words "sincerely hope that this issue can be resolved as soon as possible." Those who heard this were disappointed. The current session of the League of Nations was discussing disarmament when Japan suddenly risked the world's great disapproval and attacked China. People here heard this like a bolt from the blue. If the Executive Council does not come out to interfere and make fair sanctions, and allows the common enemy of mankind to roam free, the future of international peace is especially bleak. (Morning of the 20th)

Liaoning and Jilin

The Japanese Army Has No Intention of Withdrawing

Correspondence from Jin County: Since the League of Nations proposed that Japan withdraw its troops, the Japanese side has vigorously promoted that all Japanese troops stationed in various parts of Liaoning have been withdrawn to the South Manchurian Railway line. In fact, this is just a publicity stunt. As of now, not a single soldier has actually withdrawn from the fortresses in China that they occupy. The following is a summary of the actions after Japan declared its withdrawal, in order to show that Japan's conspiracy is in full swing.

Actively Preparing to Permanently Occupy Liaoning City: Heavy troops are still stationed in Liaoning City, and defensive works are actively being prepared near the North Gate and East Gate. Furthermore, trenches are being built at the Juliuhe Station along the Beining Road, and considerable troops are deployed there. Also, on the evening of October 2, a large number of Japanese troops took two armored trains and, under the pretext of suppressing bandits, passed through Baqibao, west of Xinmin, and seemed to be advancing westward. In addition, Japan occupied Liaoyuan with a large force and established a large-scale airfield nearby, where it repainted all the Chinese aircraft seized in Shenyang and transported them there for the purpose of bombing cities in eastern Liaoning and attacking trains. Although Japan has declared to the international community that it will withdraw its troops immediately, it is actually preparing for a long-term occupation at all times and in all places. Who would believe the so-called withdrawal?

Theft Cases Occur Repeatedly and Are Ignored: Since the provincial capital was occupied by the Japanese army, the Japanese have used cruel methods to treat our people. First, they let their soldiers plunder and rape, and then they incited Korean and Japanese ruffians to rob everywhere. They also set fire to and destroyed the Public Security Bureau, which maintained local order. In addition, on the 21st of last month, the Northeast Grain

Also, the electric force factory and the public bus factory were occupied, and all employees were expelled. Moreover, theft cases have occurred repeatedly in recent days, and the Japanese army has ignored them. As a result, the citizens are in a state of panic all day long, and businesses have not yet resumed operations.

Releasing Prisoners and Disrupting Order: In addition to the above, the Japanese are also using conspiracies everywhere to disrupt the order of our society. For example, whenever the Japanese army occupies a Chinese county town, it releases the prisoners in the prison, selecting those who have committed the most heinous crimes first. The purpose is to use these desperate people to disrupt local security and shake the Chinese regime. As for those who were imprisoned for crimes such as Ji Gong's selling of national land, not only are they released first, but they are also immediately used as their pawns. Although Japan has stated that it has not released prisoners, the facts are all there, and it cannot be allowed to quibble.

Forcibly Buying Grain with Feng Piao: In addition to releasing prisoners, Japan has recently been using large amounts of Feng Piao to buy grain in various places along the South Manchurian Railway, Shenhai Railway, Jichang Railway, and Jidun Railway. If the Chinese people are unwilling to sell, Japan will use threats and force to compel them. Under their tyranny, the Chinese people have no choice but to obey. As a result, all the new grain harvested in Northeast China this year has been bought by the Japanese. In the future, the Japanese plan to circulate gold notes in the market to completely defeat Feng Piao, in order to trap the people of Northeast China in a desperate situation. Their intention can be described as malicious.

Forcibly Building the Ji-Hui Railway: What is most alarming to us is that Japan is forcibly building the Ji-Hui Railway and using it to plunder Chinese territory. According to recent visitors from Jilin, after Japan occupied Yanji, it immediately forced Chinese farmers and workers to work day and night, actively carrying out construction. It is estimated that the Ji-Hui Railway will be completed in half a month. The Chinese people there are killed miserably if they do not obey their orders. Japan also intends to expel all the Chinese residents along the Ji-Hui Railway on the day of its completion, and then move in a large number of Koreans to carry out reclamation, turning the area into a Japanese colony. If our country's authorities do not find a way to stop it, I am afraid that the land along the Ji-Hui Railway will no longer be ours in the shortest possible time.

Li Yi Shamelessly Takes Office: In recent days, there have been organizations of civil maintenance associations in the cities of Liaoning and Jilin. Among them, there are certainly people who aim to maintain local security, but there are also many people who, under the coercion and instigation of the Japanese, rise up to act as accomplices. For example, Yuan Jinkai, Yu Chonghan, and others recently organized a local security maintenance committee in Shenyang, and Xi Qia and others organized an autonomous government in Jilin. These were purely instigated by the Japanese. The reason why Japan does this is nothing more than to use the old tricks of annexing Korea to annex our China. However, some people in our country are actually willing to be Li Wanyong, shamelessly taking pleasure in it. This is truly a great shame for our nation. However, although Yuan and others were instructed by the Japanese, they have not yet been formally appointed by the Japanese. However, it is unexpected that recently, Li Yi was formally appointed by the Japanese pseudo-Shenyang Mayor Doihara as the Director of the Shenyang Civil Affairs Office. Li Yi was originally the magistrate of Shenyang County. After Shenyang was occupied, Li was forced out by the Japanese to maintain local security. The Japanese recognized him as capable. Recently, Doihara actually appointed Li as the Director of the Shenyang Civil Affairs Office, and Li actually took office on October 1 in accordance with the order. This kind of demented and shameless act of serving the enemy is even worse than that of Yuan Yu and others. (September 4)

Recent Situation in Jilin

Most Newspapers Have Stopped Publishing

No Schools Are in Session

Correspondence from Jilin: After the Japanese army arrived in Jilin, the Jilin newspaper offices were greatly oppressed. Police Chief Tsuboi informed the newspapers that they must be inspected. The large format must be sent to the headquarters by 3:00 p.m. every day, where Tsuboi would sign it and return it. All military actions and words unfavorable to the Japanese army were not allowed. Only the Jichang Daily, a Chinese newspaper in the provincial capital, was able to publish because the large format was assembled early and there was not enough time. Therefore, only one large sheet was published, and the news only occupied one page. The rest was all advertisements. Most of the news published was not related to the current situation. Therefore, sales were greatly reduced. Foreign newspapers took advantage of the opportunity to expand greatly, and sales soared. This was inevitable. Since the situation changed, all the Chinese newspapers that dared to speak out on weekdays have stopped publishing. The extra edition of the incident.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

The Xinzhuang Chamber of Commerce Organizes a Merchant Corps: The Xinzhuang Township Chamber of Commerce in this county, recognizing the urgency of the national crisis and following the telegram from the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, convened a special temporary meeting of executive and supervisory committee members at 7:00 PM last night (the 7th) to discuss the organization of a merchant corps. The proposal was unanimously approved on the spot. Subsequently, Qian Shixin, Wang Xingsheng, Zhou Menglin, and two others were appointed as organizers responsible for all preparations. The initial funding will be temporarily borrowed from the remaining funds of the security corps and will be repaid after fundraising. Regarding firearms, the chamber of commerce will recall the fast-firing revolvers that it had lent to the fifth sub-station of the township for self-defense. The number of corps members was set at 24, to be recruited by the organizers.

Nine Criminals Executed by Firing Squad: The Songhu Pacification Zone Headquarters repeatedly received reports of the capture of bandits involved in looting incidents in Xincang, Yaqian, Zhu Jing, Xinhuang, Fu Huang, and other places. Yang Azhao, Jin Shunming (aka Jin Dongquan), Song Yaolin, Jin Heshang, Shen Yongshun (aka Shen Ahai), Zhou Quangen, Li Akai, Yu Guihu, and Huang Yougen were found guilty after interrogation. Based on the Provisional Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits, they were all sentenced to death. This was reported to the Jiangsu Pacification Commissioner's Office, which approved the execution. Commander Cao, upon receiving the telegram, signed the order to transfer the nine bandits, including Yang Azhao, on the morning of the 7th at 10:00 AM. After verifying their identities, they were bound and taken to the Yuhuangge execution ground and executed by firing squad to serve as a warning. Investigation into the Tang Surname Murder Case: Tang Zhiyao, the owner of the Tang Helong sesame oil shop at Kuatang Bridge outside the west gate of the city, was suddenly killed by a violent intruder at 2:00 AM on the night of September 5th last year. At the time, the prosecutor conducted an examination and found multiple knife wounds, indicating a brutal death. There was widespread suspicion in society that his son, Tang Qiusheng, had instigated the perpetrators. Subsequently, relatives (the deceased's younger brother) Zhigao and others strongly defended him, published an advertisement, and sent a letter to correct the rumors and dispel the misinformation. As the real killer had not been apprehended, the case was shelved. Now, after Shen Shaoqing was arrested and confessed to the murder of Tang, he identified Tang's son, Qiusheng, as the instigator. The court prosecutor's office immediately arrested Tang Qiusheng at 1:00 PM today for interrogation. The security was tight, and the details are unclear. The murderer, Shen Shaoqing, was also brought in for confrontation. It is said that the prosecutor's office will conduct a thorough investigation to reach a verdict.

Suzhou

Bands of Bandits Lurking in Taihu: Recently, banditry has resurged in the countryside of Suzhou, causing widespread panic among the villagers. Yesterday (the 8th), the county government received a report from Xu, the Chief of the Guangfu District Public Security Bureau: (1) Bandits frequently appear in areas along Taihu Lake, including Shanyanggang, Kengkengkou, Yaoshang, Tandong Township, Man, Da, and Xiao Gongshan. (2) The bandit leader Qin Banglin's gang, consisting of about 40 to 50 bandits armed with military weapons, along with gangs from Haizhou, Henan, and Jiangbei, are lurking in Taihu Lake, moving unpredictably. People throughout the lake region are startled multiple times a night. Those with some assets have moved to the city. The stationed police patrol boats are unable to navigate Taihu Lake. As winter defense approaches, preventive measures should be planned in advance. County Magistrate Wu immediately sent a letter to the third water public security district, requesting the allocation of warships for suppression. Villagers in Dongting East Mountain also submitted a request yesterday for the dispatch of troops to defend against bandits.

Financial Department Denies the Retention of Disaster Relief Funds: Various circles in Suzhou had discussed and resolved to levy an additional month's rent from the shops in the urban area starting in September, which would yield approximately 60,000 silver dollars. Half of this amount was to be retained for disaster relief and water conservancy repairs. The County Finance Bureau submitted a report to the Finance Department for record. Yesterday, instructions were received stating that the additional rent levy could proceed as planned, but the retention of half the funds was not approved. Because the provincial construction bonds had already been designated for specific purposes, it would be inappropriate to change them without a resolution from the provincial government, to avoid setting a precedent for other counties. Therefore, the request was denied.

Anti-Japanese Association Begins Inspection of Japanese Goods: The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of this county, having concluded the registration of Japanese goods at the end of September, began inspecting Japanese goods in the city and its surroundings today (the 6th). The investigators included Zha Zhi Chao, Wu Rong Jian, and Wu Mudi.

County Water Patrol Team Rescues Hostages: Xue Yong, the captain of the county water patrol team, led a team disguised as farmers on the 5th, riding on a civilian boat to suppress bandits in areas such as Shuangmiaogang in Taihu Lake. They encountered bandits, and a firefight ensued for about half an hour. The bandits then escaped by swimming. In addition to killing two bandits on the spot, they rescued Xu Wu, the daughter-in-law of Xu Jinshan from Liuxu Village outside the north gate of the city, her young son Amao, and Lu Hexiang, who had been kidnapped from Hengjing in Wuxian County, along with a boat and several stolen items. After a preliminary interrogation by Captain Xue, the female bandit confessed without denying. She has been transferred to the county for further investigation today.

Chamber of Commerce Standing Committee Requests Tax Reduction from the Provincial Government: The county's business tax is 15,000 yuan per year, which has been approved by the Finance Department for collection on behalf of the county. The chamber of commerce began collecting the tax on August 10th, and the current accounting shows that the annual amount is less than 10,000 yuan. Yesterday, the executive committee resolved to send standing committee member Wu Minyu to the provincial government to request approval for a tax reduction to alleviate the difficulties faced by businesses.

Wuxi

Director of the Construction Bureau Takes Office: Mao Feng, the director of the Construction Bureau of this county, was accused by Wang Jingqing and others last month to the provincial government. The provincial government meeting recently resolved that Director Mao should await further assignment, and the vacant position would be filled by Yao Dixing, a local from this county who previously served as the director of the bureau. After being appointed, Yao arrived at the bureau yesterday (the 8th) to take over the work and is scheduled to be formally sworn in. Meeting on the Amount of Tax Reduction for Disaster-Stricken Fields: The county government of this county, due to the severe disaster situation in various districts this year, with as many as 298,300 mu of fields submerged, convened a meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM at Wenxi Hall, bringing together the district chiefs and various departments such as party affairs, politics, public security, finance, and construction, to discuss the amount of tax reduction for the submerged fields and the methods. County Magistrate Chen presided over the meeting, and three key issues were resolved: (1) It was resolved to examine the original reports from each district regarding the submerged fields, totaling 298,300 mu. After deducting 4,000 mu, there are 236,730 mu that are completely barren and 57,569 mu that are partially barren. These fields are calculated based on the actual amount of fertile land, and the land price tax for the entire year will be waived for all completely barren fields. The tax will be reduced by 50% for partially barren fields, with 50% actually collected. All fields that have not reported barrenness will be taxed in full. (2) It was resolved that for the land price tax on barren land that should be exempted this year, some have already cleared the first installment of the land price tax, making it difficult to refund. It has now been decided that the first installment of the 20th year's land price tax will still be collected in full and offset against the first installment of the 21st year's land price tax. (3) It was resolved that in the past, the barren land registers were handled solely by the district grain brokers, which often led to extortion and many malpractices. This time, the investigation and creation of the barren land registers should be strictly supervised by the district and township chiefs. All barren land registers should be reviewed by the district and township chiefs and stamped with the seals of the district and township offices. If any grain bookkeepers are still found to be engaging in fraud or extortion, the district and township chiefs should report them to the county government and the Finance Bureau for strict investigation.

Changzhou

Police Team Captures Bandit and Transfers Him to the County: According to reports, the first squad of the first platoon of the Lao Guqiao police station in the fourth district of Wuyi County learned that a bandit named "One Foot Head" was hiding in Caojiata. They dispatched a team to search and arrested Qi Atu, the brother of "One Foot Head", who was transferred to the team for preliminary interrogation. He confessed without denying that he had conspired to extort money. The team transferred the suspect to the county for investigation on the 7th.

Anti-Japanese Association Seizes Japanese Paper: On the 7th, inspectors from the Wuyi County Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association seized a large quantity of Japanese paper at Biaochang in Ximen, including four large pieces of Qianshunxing white oil paper and one piece of red oil paper. In addition, there were also many pieces of paper materials from companies such as Tongtaichang, Deyuanchang, and Zhaoxin, which were all impounded and sealed by the Anti-Japanese Association pending disposal.

Zhenjiang

Entertainment Venues Shut Down Separately: The County Party Affairs Executive Committee held its 14th meeting yesterday to discuss the cessation of entertainment. The resolutions were: (1) A letter should be sent to the Provincial Public Security Bureau to strictly ban Qingchang venues (Chinese opera singing without makeup). (2) Movie theaters should screen patriotic films as much as possible. (3) Storytelling venues should exploit anti-Japanese materials as much as possible. (4) Beijing opera performances should be suspended. (5) A letter should be sent to the Provincial Propaganda Committee not to raise funds through entertainment activities. (6) Public banquets should be stopped.

Taixian

Nighttime Scare in Qutang Township: On the night of the 2nd of this month, a motorboat passing through Qutang Township in this county accidentally crashed into the piers of the East Bridge. Subsequently, Liu Jianqing, a committee member of the township chamber of commerce, was publicly elected to go forward to inquire. Unexpectedly, the boat, without asking the details, sent troops ashore, violently beating the person making inquiries and deploying troops along the way to cut off traffic. Order in the whole city was immediately disrupted. Afterwards, it was learned that the boat belonged to Staff Officer Zhu of the Commissioner's Office. The citizens of the township have jointly reported the facts to Commissioner Zhang, requesting that he investigate and handle the matter according to law to maintain his reputation. It is reported that people from Biao County who are in Shanghai also have a serious opinion about this matter.

Jiaxing

Specialist in Identification of Japanese Goods Arrives in He: The inspection team of the Jiaxing Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association had previously seized white sugar and various other goods at the wharf, sub-customs, post office, and station. The purchasing merchants had raised objections. The inspection team, for the sake of careful investigation, sent representatives to Shanghai to hire experts to come to He for identification. They have already accompanied Shi Gong (specializing in identifying miscellaneous goods and cloth), Sun Chunshan (specializing in identifying southern goods), and Mei Kaifu (specializing in identifying cloth, etc.), three identification experts dispatched by the Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association, to He. On the 7th, they tested the 45 bags of sugar seized at the sub-customs bag by bag, finding 5 bags of Japanese sugar and 10 bags of mixed Chinese-Japanese sugar, with the rest being Taikoo sugar. The various suspected Japanese goods sealed by the county party headquarters have been identified separately since the 8th. The Anti-Japanese Association will also dispatch personnel to jointly seal all registered Japanese goods in the shops with the Public Security Bureau Security Team, starting on the 8th. Any violations will be handled in accordance with the Zhejiang Province Provisional Rules for Punishing Treacherous Merchants Privately Transporting and Selling Japanese Goods.

Various Agencies Conduct Military Training: The entire staff of the Jiaxing County Party Headquarters is implementing military training, which has been implemented since the day before yesterday. Wang Chunong has been hired as the instructor.

Pinghu

Two Families Robbed in One Night: The home of Yin Gongmei outside the east gate was robbed on the night of the 7th. Yin was conducting chanting with monks at 11:00 pm, and seven robbers suddenly broke in with weapons. Yin's family members looked at each other in dismay, not daring to make a sound, allowing them to rummage through the boxes and loot to their hearts' content. The guests attending the memorial service were also affected. Later, they turned to the Yang family in Yangshu Village, forcing them to hand over silver. When Yang refused, they were also robbed in the same way, suffering considerable losses. They calmly left south before dawn.

Hangzhou

Zhang Nanxian Enthusiastic about Military Training: The military training for all staff of the Zhejiang Provincial Government has already begun. The departments and offices are compiled into one brigade, divided into three companies. Practical training is held every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday, and academic subjects are held every Tuesday and Thursday. They are working hard to implement the training. They have been practicing footwork in the auditorium for several days, and gun drills will be taught starting next week. Ten staff members of the Finance Department, including the elderly and weak Wei Songtang and Lu Min, were unable to cope and were allowed to retire. However, Chairman Zhang Nanxian, who is already 58 years old, is still vigorous and can be called a model for the whole group. He had already trained to the point of kneeling and preparing to fire on the morning of the day before, kneeling on the ground with the crowd, with great spirit. In addition, there is also an old staff member, Ye Jingren, who is a clerk and is already 68 years old, who also attends every day and does not want to retire.

Shaoxing

Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association Prepares to Organize Volunteer Corps: The case of organizing a volunteer corps by the Shaoxing Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association was resolved by the County Party Headquarters yesterday. Together with the county government, they will hold a fundraising meeting for the entire county's gentry and merchants and various agencies on a scheduled basis. On one hand, they will organize a preparatory office for the volunteer corps as soon as possible to solicit members. On the 6th, they gathered all staff members of party and government agencies to discuss methods of military training.

Schedule for Expanded Disguised Propaganda: Shaoxing schools are scheduled to hold expanded disguised anti-Japanese national salvation propaganda in various theaters on October 10th. The expenses are temporarily set at 150 yuan, which will be raised by the Celebration of National Day Preparatory Committee from all walks of life.

Each District Rushes to Organize Voluntary Security Corps: The Shaoxing County Government issued a notice to the heads of each township and district yesterday, stating that at a time when the country is facing multiple problems, with external troubles and internal worries, the development is still in its infancy, and the provincial security team is also concentrating, local security is of utmost importance. In addition to thoroughly reorganizing the existing security corps, they should quickly convene each important or prosperous village and try to organize voluntary security corps, collecting civilian firearms, with at least 20 members or more. They should complete the allocation and deployment within 20 days from the date of arrival of the document and intensify training to defend themselves.

Letter of Reply

Letter from the Shanghai Transport Industry Association

Recently, I read in the foreign news section of your newspaper that more than 200 pieces of Japanese goods such as foreign cloth and paper materials were seized in Suzhou, which were transported from Shanghai through Huitong and Dingtong and other transportation companies. They were immediately detained and sealed for reporting to the association, awaiting disposal. I was surprised to read this and made a long-distance telephone inquiry to the Wuxian County Association in Suzhou. It was claimed that the goods transported to Su were inspected by personnel dispatched by the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association and were found to be non-Japanese goods and were released one by one at that time, and there was no detention. The matter concerns the reputation of each company, and I am deeply afraid of rumors and hearsay. I am specifically writing to request a correction.

Special Publication

Secret Meeting in Japan to Uphold Rights and Interests in Manchuria and Mongolia

Summary Translation of Minutes

These secret meeting minutes were secretly sold to a Chinese person by Japanese ronin. Now that the Japanese are taking advantage of our disasters to occupy our Liaoning and Jilin, my close friend and executive committee member of this association, Mr. Wang Dan, who is stationed in Harbin, is concerned that the country will be destroyed at any time, so he quickly sent me these secret meeting minutes. After receiving and reading them, I realized that the time when our country is suffering from natural disasters and man-made disasters is regarded by the Japanese as a God-given opportunity. The current instructions to the restoration faction to carry out nation-building movements in Manchuria and Mongolia, and to urge bandits to endanger railway safety, are all pre-planned. As for their research on the international situation and the means of coercing and inducing our Northeast authorities, they are all extremely insidious and vicious, using the pretext of upholding their vested rights in Manchuria to achieve Japan's ultimate goal (namely, annexing Manchuria and Mongolia to complete its continental policy). Readers should not focus too much on the discussion of railway rights in the content, but should focus on their political intentions. Liu Lumin.

(1) Time: 9:00 AM to 2:00 PM on December 7th of last year. (2) Venue: Office of the Minister of Colonial Affairs. (3) Attendees: Minister of Colonial Affairs Matsuda, President Sengoku, Director Kimura, Foreign Ministry officials Yoshida and Nagai, Vice Ministers of Colonial Affairs Komura and Kosaka, participating military officials, Director of the Treaty Bureau Matsunaga, Director of the Asia Bureau, Vice Minister of the Army of the Military Department, Vice Chief of Staff, and Chief of the First Section. (4) Resolutions: (A) Sent to bring Manchuria and Mongolia's diplomatic power to Nanjing, we will take a lenient approach to the outside and a strict approach to the inside to oppose it. Furthermore, we will take the opportunity to emphasize and force them to still appoint Zhang Xueliang as the chief officer responsible for diplomacy, so that the empire can maintain its special status and privileges. (B) Take an interfering attitude towards the construction of the Feng faction's railway network to prevent its realization, especially by inducing it to coordinate with us through the strategy of forcing war and seeking peace. The restriction on the Manchuria-Mongolia railway freight rates and the cargo absorption area seems to be enough to permanently protect the prosperity of the South Manchuria Railway and Dalian Port. When the God-given opportunity comes, the empire's goals for Manchuria and Mongolia can be achieved.

Director Kimura's explanation of the proposal stated that the maverick Zhang Xueliang is rushing towards us with the momentum of ten thousand horses. He has entrusted Wang Jiazhen with his diplomacy to the south and Gao Jiyi with his railways to the north, working together to smash our special rights in Manchuria and Mongolia in one fell swoop. However, Chiang and Zhang are in the same boat... and there are two factions, new and old, within the Feng faction, who are mutually hostile... According to the efforts of our Army Staff Department to instigate a major collapse within the Feng faction, this is an inevitable certainty that can be waited and seen.

Behind Zhang Xueliang's politics, there are still more than 4,000 bandits scattered in Manchuria and Mongolia, and more than 8,000 restorationists, all of whom depend on our breath and are treated with our appeasement. In the event that the infighting within the Feng faction becomes apparent, we will merge these two forces into one, and especially add unscrupulous Koreans to them... At that time, whether we want to incline to the Luan faction or support the old faction, or even make Manchuria and Mongolia the world of the restoration faction to achieve our ideal, this can be determined according to how our national interests are. (Lu Min's note) Making Manchuria and Mongolia the world of the restoration faction is to achieve the Japanese people's ideal. What ideal is it? Even the ideal of making Manchuria and Mongolia the second Korea. I hope that the people of the country will pay attention to Japan's current violent and cruel actions, which are intended to realize the above-mentioned ideal. If bandits and restorationists recognize thieves as their fathers, their crimes cannot be forgiven, and their foolishness is also beyond reach.

The Nine-Power Treaty concluded at the Washington Conference after the European War bound the empire's free actions in Manchuria and Mongolia. If the empire were to confront it with aggressive imperialism, it would inevitably arouse misunderstandings in various countries. Because of this relationship, Manchuria-Mongolia policy must have opportunities in both international and Chinese aspects before it can be decided. It is not like the Zhang Zuolin government era, when everything can be done according to our opinion. The South Manchuria Railway sacrificed more than 200,000 people and used a total of more than 800 staff to create a register of Manchuria-Mongolia bandits and appease their leaders. All of this was to create this opportunity, and the Staff Department used the Black Dragon Society, the Patriotic Society, the Daika Society, etc., and linked them with the imperialists, just to create their opportunity. Such as specially organizing secret investigation agencies in Yingkou, Huludao, and Bei Ning Road... such as moving the authorities of Usuri and the Eastern Railway of Red Russia to cooperate with us, all of this is to promote the progress of our rights and interests. According to Nanman, make this underwater effort and sacrifice such a large amount of money, all to create a God-given opportunity for me, in order to assist my Manchuria-Mongolia policy and become a golden city and iron wall. Here it is sufficient to prove that President Sengoku is extremely eager to seek a fundamental and beneficial solution to the Manchuria-Mongolia problem, in order to establish a hundred-year plan for the country. It is clear that it is by no means as incompetent and helpless as the outside world proclaims. (Lu Min's note) Japan's resolute implementation of the Manchuria-Mongolia policy today, according to the above explanation, is because it has learned from the international financial panic and the frequent disasters in our country, the so-called arrival of the God-given opportunity, so it dares to take measures to achieve its final goal. Recently, the international atmosphere has been poor, and it has also instructed the restoration faction and bandits to recklessly sabotage. Although the Japanese are cunning, how can they cover up the eyes and ears of the world with one hand? (To be continued)

Education News

Special Publication

Respectfully Informing the Educational Community of Japanese Atrocities

(3) Shu Xincheng

Three: Spiritual Strength. I bring up the words "spiritual strength," and some will surely laugh at me as being pedantic. In reality, the reason that humans are different from other animals is that, besides material desires, there is also spiritual function. What is called the "spirit of the people" and the "national soul" are nothing more than expressions of this spiritual function. What is called a "patriot sacrificing himself for the sake of righteousness" and a "loyal minister serving his ruler and repaying the country" are all governed by this spiritual function. In China over the past 30 years, due to frequent internal unrest, the central thought and central belief that sustained the nation have been completely destroyed. Moreover, foreign aggression has been pressing hard, leading to repeated failures. The nation's confidence in stabilizing and securing the country has also gradually diminished. Today, besides increasing material strength in education, in the spiritual aspect, I, as a friend, believe that the following matters should be given at least the most attention:

A. Cultivation of Self-Confidence. China has the most ancient founding and the earliest culture. Whether from the perspective of the nation or the individual, it can be proven that our intelligence and wisdom are not inferior to others. Although in recent years the nation has been weakened due to the intertwined pressure of foreign aggression and internal unrest, this is temporary and inevitable in a transitional era (the French Revolution is a precedent). Our people should not lose heart because of this. We should have confidence in the ability to promote national glory and confidence that, through the efforts of the people, China can permanently stand tall in the world. This belief should be cultivated from history and geography textbooks. Any shallow mentality of fearing and fawning over foreigners should be driven out relentlessly (such as using English on postage stamps and store invoices, which greatly affect the national self-esteem, should not be ignored because they are small), and in practice.

B. Cultivation of the Spirit of the Rule of Law. China lacks the spirit of the rule of law due to various historical reasons. In an era of isolation, rule by people could still be self-sustaining, but now a nation cannot stand without the rule of law. This lack of spirit, on one hand, reduces solidarity and enterprising spirit, and on the other hand, increases selfishness and a desire for good luck (the current Japanese earthquake, even newspapers openly show schadenfreude, the nation's desire for good luck is completely exposed). At the same time, it is also the source of internal unrest. Educators must recognize this harm and lead by example to train young people to implement the rule of law in practice. C. Cultivation of Patriotism. The nation is where our people live and entrust their lives. The good or bad, survival or death of the nation has a close relationship with the individual. Anyone who invades our nation is invading myself. Dying for the nation and avenging the nation have the same meaning and importance as dying for an individual and avenging an individual. And the former is even more glorious than the latter because it can sacrifice the small self to protect the big self. This meaning is now rarely mentioned. The educational community, because "politics is a hot potato," even avoids saying the word "nation." However, "everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the world." At this critical moment of national crisis and survival, how can the far-sighted educational community sit idly by? Cultivating a generous and united patriotic heart in young people is a priority in current education.

Local News

Resolutions of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation of the Educational Community

Plan for Economic Severance with Japan

Guiding Principles for Anti-Japanese National Salvation

The Shanghai Educational Community National Salvation Federation held its second city-wide representatives' conference yesterday afternoon at 3:00 p.m. at Wuben Girls' School, Xiaoximen. It resolved to pass four important cases, including the guiding principles for anti-Japanese national salvation, a concrete plan for economic severance with Japan, and various important matters such as regulations. The details of the meeting are recorded below:

Representatives Present: Representatives from various schools attended yesterday, including Chen Gonglu from the Sino-French Institute of Technology, Li Zhaoshi from Jiaotong University, Hu Shuhua from Tongji University, Chu Fucheng from the Law School, Ou Yuanhuai from Daxia University, Gao Renou from Tongde School, Guo Qiyuan from Jiannan Hospital, Sun Xiangyuan from Soochow University, Cheng Xin from Wusong Middle School, Cai Yan from the YMCA Middle School, Zhang Yiceng from Datong University, Xu Peikun from Central University, Wan Rong from Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School, Yang Weiyu from the Chinese Vocational Education Society, Zheng Xiwang from Shanghai High School, Wang Xiaoying from Wuben Girls' School, and other representatives from major and minor schools, about 400 people.

Meeting Proceedings: The meeting began at 3:00 p.m. with Hu Shuhua and Jiang Wenyu reporting on the work progress of the Executive Committee. Then, Hu Shuhua reported on the process of petitioning in Guangdong, and Zhang Mupin, a professor from Northeastern Fengyong University, reported on the destruction of Fengyong University. Following this, various cases were discussed and various plans were passed. The meeting adjourned at 6:30 p.m.

Important Resolutions: Four important resolutions were passed yesterday, including: (1) A resolution to send a telegram to Zhang Xueliang, setting a deadline for investigating the whereabouts of Fengyong. It was resolved to pass the telegram to the Executive Committee for handling. (2) A resolution to curb the opportunistic price increases of domestic goods. It was resolved that the Executive Committee should suggest that various anti-Japanese associations handle the matter. (3) A resolution to promote the organization of anti-Japanese national salvation associations in the national educational community. It was resolved to hand it over to the Executive Committee for handling. (4) Review of slogans: it was resolved to retain them. Plan for Economic Severance with Japan: (A) Economic severance with Japan covers a wide range and involves many methods. However, not using Japanese goods is actually the most important method among various methods. This plan is specifically aimed at this simple goal, and the effectiveness of previous boycotts of Japanese goods is difficult to determine. Judging from the number of imported goods in the Customs trade register, the effect is quite small. Therefore, some people inevitably have doubts about this matter. In fact, the previous efforts were not great, all because the handling was not good. The reason why the handling was not good was because of the lack of "methods." This time, it is not difficult to be at the forefront. Everyone's conscience is aroused, and of course, people cannot be judged by normal reasoning. The plan must be perfect, the organization must be precise, the application must be appropriate, and the progress must be swift, which is also related to the issue of methods. Based on past experience, learning from past mistakes, we should gather multiple wisdom and discuss methods that have fewer drawbacks and more benefits, in order to first try it out in the Shanghai educational community. (B) In order to ensure that this plan can be implemented permanently and effectively, the following three principles are listed: (1) The scope should be expanded. (2) The time should be sustained. (3) The research should be precise. Taking it a step further, the nature of Japanese goods is classified into the following three categories, and three people from each university's business and engineering departments will conduct research on them one by one: (1) Those that can be replaced by existing domestic goods. (2) Those that can be dispensed with. (3) Those that can be manufactured ourselves. (C) Once the principles are established, further details and methods are discussed: (1) The association will prepare and print a pledge form (with a vow) for distribution to various schools. The vows are: 1. I resolve not to use Japanese goods. 2. My family members resolve not to use Japanese goods. 3. I will advise my relatives and friends not to use Japanese goods. (2) All pledgers should purchase a badge after filling out the pledge form and wear it all day long to show their determination. This badge will be produced by the association on behalf of the pledgers, with each badge priced at seven cents. At the time, each school and organization can contact the distribution for as many as they need. (3) After receiving the pledge form, each school and organization should convene a general meeting of all faculty, staff, and students to explain the three major principles of not using Japanese goods and the methods for filling out the pledge form and purchasing and wearing badges. The reasons for filling out the pledge form and badges must also be explained in detail. (4) When convening the general meeting, each school and organization should also propose the following two matters and agree to implement them: (1) Use the method of ten-person groups, with each person responsible for separately pledging nine people to fill out the form, purchase the badge, and not use Japanese goods. After the group is complete, report to the person in charge of the school or organization, collect the pledge forms, submit them, and prepare the price to receive the badges and wear them. In addition, the other nine people should continue to seek comrades in this way. The more you promote, the wider it can be spread. The procedures for taking the pledge form and purchasing the badge can be handled by the original person in charge to contact the relevant agency. (2) Among the people in each school and organization, those who can undertake part or all of the research work can form groups on their own and handle investigation, editing, suggestions, publicity, advocacy, liaison, assistance, and other matters in their spare time. (5) Each school and organization must designate one or two staff members of this agency to be responsible for handling this matter. (6) After the Executive Committee of the Association resolves and approves the funding for this case, in addition to notifying the schools and organizations present to implement it as appropriate, it will also try to promote it to other agencies and organizations, hoping that they will all adopt it.

Guiding Principles for Anti-Japanese National Salvation: (1) The Necessary Understanding of Anti-Japanese National Salvation: 1. Japan's active policy of invading Manchuria and Mongolia. 2. The causes of Japan's invasion of our country. 3. The process of Japan's invasion of our country. 4. The current situation of Japan's invasion of our country's Northeast. 5. The geographical situation of our country's Northeast. 6. The current situation after the Meiji Restoration in Japan. (2) The Necessary Spirit of Anti-Japanese National Salvation: 1. Vow to avenge the shame and save the country with wisdom, courage, loyalty, and trustworthiness. 2. Define avenging the shame and revenge as the goal of anti-Japanese severance efforts. 3. To always not cooperate with Japan and sever economic relations. 4. Develop a spirit of hard work, diligence, self-improvement, and unyielding. 5. To have the determination to study hard and save the country with diligent study. 6. To have the will to strive for progress and cultivate personality and morality. (3) The Work of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement: 1. Regarding military training: A. In accordance with the Central Regulations on the Education Outline for Volunteer Soldiers, schools should organize student volunteer soldiers and juvenile volunteer soldiers. B. Implement military training and exercise physical fitness. C. Train female students with knowledge and skills in nursing, rescue, telecommunications, etc. D. Schools should jointly organize a central agency for unified command and training. E. Volunteer soldiers should absolutely obey discipline. F. Volunteer soldiers should permanently wear blue cloth with white characters on their left arm: "Unite, Struggle, Avenge Shame, Save the Country." 2. Regarding economic severance: (A) Teachers, students, and workers in schools should absolutely not use Japanese goods. (B) Teachers and students in schools should advise their families and friends to sever ties with Japan and not use Japanese goods forever. (C) Conduct a thorough investigation of Japanese goods trademarks and product names, and issue them to the public to jointly boycott Japanese goods. (D) Investigate the state of domestic industries. (E) Investigate domestic goods trademarks and product names. (F) Teachers and students swear to use domestic goods. (G) Persuade the public to use domestic goods. 3. Regarding research: (A) Research on Japanese issues and international relations. (B) Research on the Manchuria and Mongolia issues and Japan's aggressive continental policy. (C) Research on the relationship between national defense terrain and military defense. (D) Research on thorough measures for economic severance with Japan. (E) Research on practical methods for promoting domestic goods. 4. Regarding publicity: (A) Promote national peace and unity to jointly resist foreign enemies, avenge shame, and revenge. (B) Urge the government to announce severance with Japan. (C) Ask the government to pay attention to national defense and quickly send troops to recover lost territory. (D) Awaken the public to unanimously resist Japan and be the government's backing. (E) Intensify international publicity to make the people of all countries understand the truth. (F) Teachers and students organize anti-Japanese national salvation propaganda teams, with each team limited to five people, to conduct open-air speeches and costumed speeches. (G) Publicize to the public that Japan is the greatest enemy in their lives. (H) Make the public deeply aware that they must endure hardship and vow to avenge shame and save the country.

Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation of University Students

The 13th Meeting of Cadres

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation of University Students in this city held its 13th cadre meeting at the Youth Propaganda Corps, Xiaonanmen, yesterday afternoon at 2:00 p.m. Those present included Cao Peizi from Guanghua University, Ping Zuren from Jinan University, Gu Duanwu from Jiangnan College, Xu Guanbin from Daxia University, Zhang Shousong from the Law School, Chen Yuejiang from the Sino-French Institute of Technology, Lu Xizhen from Fudan University, Zheng Dingying from Chizhi College, Zhang Kunyu from Datong University, Duan Bojun from China Public School, Chu Fucheng, the joint representative of the university presidents, Tao Baichuan, the representative of the City Party Department, Xu Guanbin, the chairman, and Cao Peizi, the recorder. However, military training is not a problem of suspension, but the premise is that students can truly be trained. Secondly, the problems that arise are courses, playgrounds, instructors, guns, etc. President Liu Zhanen of Shanghai University said that regarding military training, the central government has already discussed a comprehensive approach. Secretary-General Jin Tong of Fudan University said that military training is very important at the moment and can make students' lives disciplined. (5) Shanghai Law School reported that it had recently discovered a reactionary declaration issued by the federation's petition delegation. (6) Various departments reported the allocation of duties: A. Director of the General Affairs Department (Daxia), Document (Guanghua), Accounting (Jiaotong University), Communication (Fudan), General Affairs (Law School) (B) Director of the Military Training Department (Jinan), other departments have not yet been assigned. (7) Motions: (A) Motion to suspend classes for half a day after Friday for military training for five weeks. It was resolved to pass the proposal in accordance with the principles proposed by the Law School. Each school must have at least two hours and no more than four hours of military training per day. There are still cases of transfer from the same school, disputes between the Law and Political Science College, etc.

Chizhi and Jiaotong Universities Officially Resume Classes

Chizhi College, both the university and middle school departments, had previously suspended classes for a day due to rampant rumors and students leaving the school. Recently, after repeated explanations from the authorities, classes resumed as usual yesterday. All students who left the school will be considered as absent. All students of Jiaotong University have resumed classes and issued a declaration, one paragraph of which says, "The past anti-Japanese national salvation work is necessary in the process, but it is a stopgap measure and temporary. We now believe that it is necessary to end it. This does not mean that we will not participate in the national salvation movement in the future, but that the method of participation should change. From the results of this petition, we can see that the government has a final determination on Japan. What we should prepare for is to prepare for a declaration of war against Japan. Because of the above reasons, we are now intensifying military training to be reserve soldiers. At the same time, we use our special training to have those who study civil engineering add the study of military defense and demolition engineering, those who study electrical engineering add the study of military transportation engineering, power grids and radio, those who study mechanical engineering add the study of repairing gun engineering, those who study chemistry add the study of military chemistry courses, those who study mathematics and physics add the study of ballistics and meteorology, those who study management add the study of military transport engineering. We each do our best to prepare for a declaration of war. We are definitely not ignoring national affairs because of attending classes, but preparing for the work of declaring war on Japan by attending classes. At the same time, we are still continuing our publicity work. When necessary, we are prepared to sacrifice our studies and strike."

Nanyang Business School Does Not Suspend Classes Due to Rumors

The rumors in Zhabei two days ago caused widespread panic. The Nanyang Commercial Senior Middle School on Tiantong'an Road happened to be adjacent to the Japanese Naval Headquarters. All the students gathered and held an emergency meeting. First, Li Dongqing, the captain of the student volunteer army, spoke, saying that students should remain calm and not be swayed by rumors, nor should they rely on the concession for shelter. All the students were united in their determination to coexist and die with the school in case of misfortune, so they continued to attend classes as usual in recent days.

Gold Price Sees Slight Increase Again

The market situation is fluctuating and uncertain. Yesterday, the 8th, the benchmark gold price changed unpredictably, the situation was complicated and difficult to ascertain. The morning market hovered around 700 taels, while the afternoon market was often above 700 taels. There were a total of 18 taels of fluctuations throughout the day. As a result, the price rose by more than six taels, the market was turbulent, and people were unsettled, as if they were in a fog. Transactions were also varied. The price rose at the beginning of the morning, due to large orders expecting further increases that did not materialize. However, sellers were quick to react and took a downward turn, suddenly dropping to 691-692 taels. Furthermore, the exchange rate started to show deficits. Later, the US dollar exchange rate contracted and the internal market stabilized, especially as various firms were eager to buy, causing a rapid surge of more than ten taels, almost reaching 710 taels. However, there was much confusion in between, with prices rising and falling from time to time. The afternoon market was relatively calm, with little fluctuation. Observing the situation, the future is still subject to change.

At the beginning of the morning, the opening price jumped by 7 taels and 2 qian, to 704.5 taels. Silver bars remained the same, while US silver rose by 3/8. Transactions were sparse and did not cause any significant movement. Next was 705 taels. Unexpectedly, Fengyongfu, Changhengchang, Yongtong, and Taichang and others dumped their holdings, immediately driving the price downstream, breaking the 700 tael barrier. Securities

Bond Market Had Major Reversal Yesterday

Afternoon Market Soars, Trading Halted

Market Sentiment Suddenly Improves, Various Parties Aggressively Buy in at Low Prices

Many November Contracts Opened, Market Conditions Improve

Yesterday (8th), the bond market conditions at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange saw relatively few spot transactions despite several types opening for trading. Many November contracts were opened for trading, and market conditions improved, with buying and selling becoming more active, as there were significant changes in various prices. In recent weeks, the serious impact of the diplomatic situation with Japan has caused widespread anxiety. The major national floods this summer, and the prolonged failure to resolve the Guangdong issue, have also made people hesitant to invest in bonds, leading to a sharp decline of over 10-20 yuan in bond prices over the past two weeks. This excessive decline was due to the weakness of market sentiment. Once market sentiment stabilized, the reaction was inevitably strong. Observing the trend of yesterday's bond market prices, the buying interest was already active in the morning, with aggressive buying at low prices. However, there was still a general sense of hesitation, resulting in some prices rising and others falling, creating a very chaotic situation. The second half of the day saw stronger gains, with issues such as the 20-year customs bonds, consolidated tax bonds, and salt tax bonds rising significantly. In the afternoon, news spread that the diplomatic situation was turning around, and that peace in Guangdong could be achieved soon. As a result, market sentiment improved significantly, and buying interest was strong. Various bonds then saw demand exceed supply, rising four yuan higher than the previous day's registered price, leading to a halt in trading. The November contracts also rose four yuan higher than the initial opening in the morning, leading to a halt in trading. Only a few issues, such as the consolidated six customs bonds, demobilization bonds, and 96 bonds, did not reach the trading halt. It is important to note that the overall bond market situation is still not optimistic. However, if the diplomatic situation does not worsen, there is hope for continued stability. The total spot trading for the day was 20,000 yuan, and the total futures trading was 13,750,000 yuan.

Yarn and Cotton

Chaotic Yarn Market Situation

The yarn market rose in the morning and fell in the afternoon, but the trend remained chaotic and inconsistent, leading to market uncertainty. However, based on current calculations, the price of coarse yarn is still not cheaper than local yarn. Only fine yarn is cheaper than Shanghai yarn, causing the market sentiment to suddenly loosen.

Cotton Market Suddenly Turns Downward

The cotton market turned downward because most people expected American cotton to have an active upward trend, but now the telegrams show a decline of 10 British pounds, and the strong upward momentum suddenly weakened. In general, there is too much bottom stock, and the selling price of foreign cotton is still low, making it difficult for the market to be very good. Also, the gold market has a downward trend, so manufacturers are still buying foreign cotton and selling domestic cotton. The Hankou gang is also closing out its long positions, and the future is still difficult to be optimistic about.

Hankou Market Suddenly Drops by 5 Qian: The Hankou market opened in the morning, and the American cotton market fell, making the market sentiment very weak, with prices falling by 2-3 qian across all months. The afternoon was even weaker, with prices falling by 2-4 qian across all months. The total transaction volume for the day was 155,100 dan. According to the data, Jifeng sold 8,500 dan, Shenchang sold 6,800 dan, Yuande sold 6,900 dan, Xincheng sold 7,000 dan, Tianjiang sold 3,200 dan, Tongxing sold 2,600 dan, Zhenda sold 3,700 dan, and Changhe sold 2,900 dan. American Cotton Declines by 10 Points

British and Indian Cotton Both See Gains

Yesterday, American cotton was initially firm due to positive news about the political situation and the closing of short positions, but later weakened, with futures falling 8-11 British pounds and spot prices falling 10 British pounds. British cotton futures rose 8 points and spot prices rose 13 points. Egyptian cotton spot prices rose 15 points. Indian cotton was initially firm due to short covering and purchases by brokers, but later weakened due to sales by Japanese traders, with Pingguoer rising 3 rupees, Aomula rising 4.75 rupees, and Bairoxi rising 3.75 rupees. The River Rice Market is Tight and Then Slack

Yesterday, over 30 firms arrived from the river, and the appetite of urban and rural stores was increasingly weak. Transactions were minor, and the price of old rice fell by 3 jiao. As Qingming Festival is approaching, it is feared that it will be difficult to turn the situation around. New Yangdu sharp goods were still sold sporadically, and transactions were few. The market followed the downward trend. Glutinous rice was in short supply.

Flour Mills Mostly Halt Sales in the Afternoon Market

Total Transaction Value Reaches 3.4 Million

The flour market situation in the morning after the market opened. Influenced by the wheat market, the downward trend was stronger. In the short term, there were many big longs who went back to sell. In the long term, the factory side sold the goods. In the end, the price fell within 1.9 qian this month. The long-term price was slightly above 5 points. In the afternoon, the factory side stopped selling. There was also a rush to buy the recent products, and some short-term gains were made to make up for the imminent gains. The prices were raised at 3.5 points respectively. The closing price was 1 tael and 2.5 qian for October, 5 li for all the big months in November and December, no change in January, 7.5 qian for all the small months in February and March. Yesterday's flour delivery transaction was very prosperous. The total transaction volume in the upper and lower markets was 3.4 million, which is rare in recent years.

Lowest Price Found in Wheat Market

Future Market Expected to Rebound with Suspension of Auctions Due to Emergency Meeting

After yesterday's wheat market opened, continuing the weak trend from the previous day, opening prices immediately dropped by five to six cents. Furthermore, foreign wheat was quoted at a low of 34 cents. New shipments of Russian wheat were also fixed at 3.225 taels per ship, along with the continued arrival of American wheat for bidding, all of which posed a threat to the market. This triggered increased selling by large short sellers. Large long sellers were forced to sell due to margin calls, causing the market to fall repeatedly, dropping from 1 cent to 0.79 cents. The current month even reached a low of 3.224 taels, a price unseen for many years. Subsequently, short covering occurred, stabilizing market prices slightly. At the close of the market, the current month was down 0.07 cents, November down 0.04 cents, December down 0.03 cents, January down 0.05 cents, February down 0.06 cents, and March down 0.05 cents. In the afternoon, due to margin calls not being fully met and an emergency meeting being convened, auctions were suspended, it was said.

Sugar Market

Trade Begins in Raw and White Sugar for Next Year's Delivery

Taikoo Sugar Opens with 10,000 Bags

Yesterday's sugar market saw no significant rise or fall in spot sugar prices in Cuba, New York, and Java, according to telegrams from producing regions. Trading in the guild market remained sparse. Dutch No. 24 raw white sugar was still priced at 11.4 taels for new goods and 11.5 taels for high-quality goods. No. 20 medium raw white sugar was priced at 11 taels, and high-quality goods at 11.1 taels. The market situation was generally stable. Taikoo Sugar's ZB mark was priced at 12.3 taels and was in short supply upon leaving the warehouse, showing a firming trend. DY mark was priced at 12.2 taels, HX mark at 12.1 taels, and HM mark at 11.75 taels. Although transactions were few, the market outlook remained firm. 10,000 bags of dumped goods, to be shipped at the end of this month, DY mark, were priced at 8.2 taels. Remaining lots were offered and pushed at increased prices, proving quite popular. Shunjinlong sold 300 tons of dumped Dutch raw white sugar for shipment in February and March of next year at a price of 5.6 Dutch guilders. At the same time, Huaxinhao also sold 600 tons at the same price. Market sentiment was still strong, marking the first deals for next year's goods, it was said.
