Local News

National Day Commemoration Tomorrow

In the Midst of Flood Disaster and National Crisis

Extravagant Celebrations Are Inappropriate

Only Commemorative Ceremonies Will Be Held

The Municipal Executive Committee, having received instructions from the Central Government that, given the severity of the flood disaster and the ongoing national crisis, extravagant celebrations are inappropriate, yesterday specifically notified all sectors that, in addition to the customary day off, a commemorative meeting will be held at 10:00 AM on October 10th in the auditorium of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. All other entertainment and banquets must be suspended. It is said that the presidium of the meeting has been tentatively determined to consist of Tao Baichuan, Wang Xiaolai, Chen Kecheng, Fu Dewei, Zhu Yingpeng, Zhu Youhuan, and Jiang Yi.

Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement Developments

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Declares Perseverance and Unyielding Spirit

Labor Unions Declare Resolution Not to Stop

Anti-Japanese Association Declares Fundraising for National Salvation

Chinese Employees of Guangdong Maru Steamer Resign

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Issues a Declaration

Unyielding to Power Until the Goal Is Achieved

Steadfastness and Endurance Are the Only Path to Success

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday issued a declaration regarding the anti-Japanese national salvation movement, stating: "Since the Japanese military forcefully occupied the provinces of Liaoning and Jilin, they have intensified their actions, deploying troops and dispatching warships to threaten our coastal areas. Their intentions are clear: to destroy our country and enslave our people. Compatriots across the nation, having reached the limit of their endurance, have risen up to save the country, acting swiftly and speaking in unison. Since this Chamber convened a general membership meeting and resolved to sever relations with Japan, various industries have spontaneously and thoroughly engaged in boycotts of Japanese goods. From resolution to action, for several days, they have been conducting self-organized inspections, encouraging each other, making final decisions, and planning for the long term. However, rumors are circulating that the Japanese side is threatening and imposing restrictions. It should be known that patriotism is the duty of every citizen, and there are no regulations forcing people to buy. We cannot force others to buy our goods, nor can others force us to buy theirs. This principle is clear and needs no further explanation. We only hope that the merchants and people of our city will continue to uphold the spirit of steadfastness and sincerity, vowing to never forget their determination. They must understand the immense responsibility of saving the country and the nation, enduring hardship and toil, persevering with unwavering resolve, and never yielding to power until the final goal is achieved. They must abandon the habits of superficiality and exaggeration, seeking only incremental progress. It takes ten years to grow a tree, let alone succeed in saving the country. Steadfastness and endurance are the only path. We issue this sincere declaration, hoping for mutual encouragement."

All Municipal

Labor Unions Issue a Solemn Declaration

The Anti-Japanese Movement Will Not Stop as Long as the Brutal Japanese Army Does Not Withdraw

Shanghai News Agency reports: The city's postal workers' union, publishing industry union, six district water and electricity industry union, four district cigarette industry union, five district cigarette industry union, one district water and electricity industry union, seven district cotton textile industry union, pharmaceutical industry union, shipbuilding industry union, and 85 other labor unions, yesterday issued a declaration stating: "Since the Wan incident occurred, malicious assaults have targeted Chinese people. Our countrymen, suffering deeply, have cried out in agony, seeking justice and the triumph of reason. However, the brutal Japanese, using the Nakamura incident as a pretext, destroyed our South Manchuria Railway and launched a full-scale invasion. The flames of their poisonous ambitions spread everywhere, turning tens of millions of compatriots in the Eastern Provinces into slaves, and turning tens of thousands of miles of Liaoning and Jilin into territories that are no longer ours. Our people are weeping tears of blood, enduring and seeking international arbitration in the hope that the brutal Japanese will restrain themselves. For over two weeks, this Association has responded to the urgent demands and been driven by conscience, mindful that the rise and fall of the nation is the responsibility of every individual, and that in the face of national peril, we must rise together to survive. From the Anti-Japanese Aid to Overseas Chinese Association to the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, we have resolutely severed relations with Japan in order to destroy the fatal enemy, the Japanese invaders, who are irreconcilable with us. Since the implementation of these measures, the results have been significant. This is a manifestation of the awakening of conscience and the collective self-reliance of our entire nation, and we find it very gratifying. However, on the 6th of this month, the cruel Japanese actually warned our government to stop the anti-Japanese national salvation movement and dispatched a large number of warships to China to demonstrate their power. Alas, our countrymen, after being slowly tortured to near death, are still not allowed to groan. What era in human history has seen such cruelty? It is our duty to pledge our determination that as long as the brutal Japanese army does not withdraw and cease all acts of aggression, our anti-Japanese national salvation movement will not cease for a single day. We hope that all compatriots across the country, at this critical juncture when a knife is at our throats, will contribute their ideas, unite together, and obey the unified command of the government to fight a life-or-death battle with the brutal Japanese, so that we can restore our territory and preserve our sovereignty. We humbly present our humble opinions for your consideration."

Anti-Japanese Sentiment Amidst Shipping News

Chinese Employees of Japanese Steamships Resign: Many Chinese managers of Japanese commercial firms in Japan have resigned. Our local Osaka Company also received a telegram from Hong Kong yesterday stating that on the Guangdong Maru steamer of the company's Hong Kong and Keelung branches, all the lower-ranking Chinese crew members had resigned to the Japanese this time the ship arrived in Hong Kong. Sailors and stokers also left the ship en masse, nearly rendering the ship unable to sail. Later, it was able to sail after temporarily hiring foreigners in Hong Kong. This is the first ship where Chinese maritime workers have refused to cooperate with the Japanese.

Nisshin Employee Beaten: Nisshin Company recently had a batch of goods transported to Qingdao. Fearing that unloading would be impossible if shipped on their own company's vessel, they switched to a British ship for export. As usual, they sent a Chinese employee, Zhang Wenqing, to the Taikoo Company to obtain the bill of lading. Upon arriving in front of Taikoo, he was recognized by colleagues from a customs brokerage, who tried to dissuade him. When he refused, the customs brokers dragged Zhang down and beat him. After being beaten, Zhang sought help from the Taikoo taipan, an Englishman, who said that since this was a patriotic movement, foreigners should not interfere. Later, a Japanese employee from Nisshin arrived and took Zhang back to the company.

Continued Arrival of Students and Overseas Chinese: Yesterday, more students and overseas Chinese returned home on the Shanghai Maru steamer, including Zheng Renli, Yu Xunhan, Li Shengmeng, and 130 others. 49 others, including Li Gengfu, Li Jinzong, and Yang Shunli, returned home on the Maya Maru steamer. 26 others, including Zhu Shunlin and Lin Zhirong, arrived in Shanghai on the Mikasa Maru steamer. Most of the overseas Chinese were women and children. More are expected to arrive in the coming days.

Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association

Declaration for Fundraising for National Salvation

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association yesterday issued a declaration stating: "Alas, China is plagued by natural disasters and man-made calamities, and the people are struggling to survive. The brutal Japanese are taking advantage of this opportunity to carry out aggression. The occupation of Liaoning and Jilin is not enough; they are deploying troops and dispatching warships to exert their threats. Their intentions are clear: to achieve their so-called conquest of Manchuria and Mongolia in order to dissect our entire country of China. Anyone with blood in their veins cannot endure this any longer. Now, compatriots across the country are rising up to resist Japan, united as one, and not looking back. Volunteer armies are beginning to be recruited, international propaganda is being actively pursued, and economic severance is vowed for eternity. However, there are myriad ways to save the country, and economics is the key. The representatives of all sectors of this city have resolved that from today onwards, fundraising for national salvation will begin. All Chinese banks, money shops, and trust companies in this city have the obligation to collect donations. Each bank, money shop, and trust company must affix its seal or have the deputy manager sign and seal each receipt as proof and must not refuse to collect. They must report to this association every ten days for publication in the newspapers. Every little bit helps, and people should sacrifice their wealth to relieve the national crisis. Alas, our compatriots, our beloved compatriots, if you do not want to see your country perish in your lifetime, if you do not want to be slaves and beasts of burden, if you do not want your children and grandchildren to be slaughtered and trampled upon, then today is the time to generously donate. The people of Korea shared a kitchen knife among three households, and even speaking in groups of three or five was subject to interference. When they finally realized the tragedy of losing their country and their homes, it was too late to sacrifice their lives and donate their wealth. When the nest is overturned, no egg remains unbroken. Saving the country is saving oneself. We implore the nation with nine prostrations. Our fathers, brothers, uncles, siblings, sisters, why do you not come forth?"

Anti-Japanese Efforts in Various Sectors

Printing Industry Establishes Inspection Team: The Printing Industry Association convened a meeting of representatives yesterday to discuss national salvation. It was decided on the spot to formally establish a printing industry inspection team, effective immediately, and to notify members to unanimously refrain from importing Japanese goods. Any existing Japanese goods must be reported to the association immediately for verification and sealing.

Seafood Industry Seals Japanese Goods: The Seafood and Sundries Industry Association convened a general membership meeting yesterday, chaired by Ge Weian. After reporting on the inspection work of recent days, the discussion items were presented. The following six proposals were passed by the entire body: (1) All committee members, along with inspectors, will immediately set out to inspect and seal Japanese goods from members. (2) Regardless of whether or not the Japanese goods found at members' businesses have been registered with the Anti-Japanese Association, they will be sealed by this association and reported to the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association for disposition. (3) A stamp with the phrase "Forever Economically Severed from Japan" must be affixed to invoices to demonstrate resolve. (4) A notice will be sent to each business soliciting volunteer inspectors for this association. (5) A notice will be sent to each business asking those willing to serve in the National Salvation Volunteer Army to register with the National Salvation Volunteer Army Recruiting Office of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. (6) Representatives of each business will submit sworn statements. It has also been reported that, in order to demonstrate its determination to resist Japan and save the country, the Seafood and Sundries Industry Association sent a telegram to Japanese merchants some days ago, severing relations with Japan immediately and requesting them to return to their country as soon as possible. The association has received replies and is currently winding down operations in preparation for returning home in the coming days.

Japanese Hope to

Use Military Force to Suppress Anti-Japanese Movement

According to Japanese sources yesterday, the Japanese government has now decided that troops will not be withdrawn on the 14th of this month. Japanese military officers have also openly made statements about overthrowing the League of Nations. The Japanese navy is now acting in unison with the army, taking active measures. Four Japanese warships arrived some days ago, and more warships, aircraft, armored vehicles, and over-mountain guns are being transferred to Shanghai from Sasebo, as if preparing for war against us. It is unknown how our country's authorities will respond. The information known is reported separately below.

Tokiwa Battleship to Arrive in China Today: The Japanese Navy

Ministry has ordered the Sasebo Naval Base to have three ships, the 2nd-class coastal defense ship Tokiwa, the Izumo, and the special service ship Notoro, load 400 marines onto the Tokiwa starting on the 6th. The remaining two ships will be loaded with armored gun carriages, military supply trucks, military aircraft, and military supplies to sail to Shanghai. Our local source confirmed yesterday that the Tokiwa has completed loading the marines and will depart first today. The Izumo and others will follow immediately. The marines will disembark upon arrival in Shanghai, and the aircraft and gun carriages will also be moved to land for the purpose of intimidating the Chinese. Mitsui Wharf has prepared for the ship to moor.

Momo and Hinoki Depart for the Yangtze Yesterday: Commander Tanaka Osamu of the Japanese 24th Fleet and the commander of the First Overseas Detachment stationed in Shanghai jointly decided that the Momo and Hinoki would leave Shanghai yesterday morning and head to Zhenjiang and Daye. Each ship carried 50 sailors and was transferred to the command of the First Overseas Detachment after entering the river yesterday morning. The Kashi and Yanagi will remain in Shanghai.

Mayor Zhang's Remarks

Mayor Zhang Qun returned to Shanghai from Nanjing last night (the 8th) at 11:00 PM. Reporters met him on the train and asked three questions: (1) What important report did the Mayor make to the central government on this trip, and what important tasks will he undertake after returning to Shanghai? The Mayor replied, "I have not been to Nanjing for some time because the municipal government is busy. I took the opportunity to travel there because Commander Xiong returned to Shanghai to meet President Chiang and report on the security situation in Shanghai. There were no important matters to report. After returning to Shanghai, I have no special mission." The reporters then asked: (2) It is heard that the students of the Central University in Nanjing have resolved to stage a general strike. Is this true? The Mayor replied, "There are many rumors in Shanghai, which have been transmitted to the capital. Students are deeply patriotic and extremely agitated, believing that the time has come to give up their pens and take up arms. Therefore, there was a resolution to stage a general strike. However, it has recently become clear that the rumors are untrue, and the talk of a general strike has been canceled. I heard that students from Central University had sent representatives to Shanghai to contact various schools. I hope that schools in Shanghai will not spread misinformation and cause disturbances." The reporters then asked: (3) What is the situation in Guangdong? The Mayor replied, "Chen Mingshu will arrive in Shanghai today, accompanied by Li Wenfan, Gu Mengyu, Huang Huabiao, and others. When they will go to Nanjing after arriving in Shanghai will be known after we meet. I have not heard anything about the rumors that a preparatory meeting will be held in Shanghai first."

Overseas Representatives Attending the Fourth National Congress

Conversations in Shanghai en Route to Beijing

The Nation Should Consider the Root Cause When Resisting Violent Japan

Overseas representatives attending the Fourth National Congress Wu Zhaohai, Wu Mingchao, Wu Shichao, and Li Ciwen (all from British territories) arrived in Shanghai yesterday and registered at the office. As of yesterday, a total of 33 representatives had arrived, with 19 having already proceeded to Beijing. Additionally, Wang Canfen, a representative from the French branch, and Mo Yao, a representative from London, departed for Beijing yesterday morning on a special express train. Representatives from the Canadian branch and the Toronto-based Xinghua Daily, Wang Guanying and Guan Zhushi, expressed their opinions to reporters from the Xinsheng News Agency yesterday regarding their return to the country to attend the Fourth National Congress and their thoughts after the Japanese invasion of Liaoning. They stated that when they were in the United States, they were deeply concerned upon hearing about the formation of a separate government in Guangdong, the rampant activities of the "Red bandits" in Hubei and Jiangxi, and the various difficulties caused by floods. Therefore, their greatest hope for this return to the country is the peace and unity of the nation. They hope that the comrades in Guangdong can treat each other with sincerity, so that they can unite internally, put politics on the right track, and jointly resist external aggression, thereby slightly curbing the ambitions of the enemy. As for all internal disputes within the party, they hope that they can be resolved by the public at the Fourth National Congress. Secondly, overseas Chinese, due to the impact of the global economic downturn, have seen their businesses abroad greatly affected, and many intend to invest in China to develop the country's industries. However, due to the ever-changing political situation in China and the failure to completely eliminate the "Red bandits," many are taking a wait-and-see approach. If China can be unified soon, it will surely attract enthusiastic investment from overseas compatriots. This is their second mission in returning to the country. In addition, overseas compatriots are even more eager for China to be unified soon because they are treated harshly by local countries due to China's weakness. They also stated that upon hearing the shocking news of the Japanese invasion of Liaoning, they conducted investigations in Japan and felt that the arrogance of the Japanese made people feel uncomfortable everywhere. What was particularly painful was that the Japanese newspapers propagated to their people that "there is no need to be surprised by the economic severance of relations with China; it will take no more than five minutes at most." At the same time, the Japanese told Chinese compatriots returning to China, "Why do you need to return to China? Japan can completely occupy China within three days and will definitely capture you and imprison you on the top of Mount Fuji." Therefore, their personal opinion is that to resist the Japanese, one must consider the root cause. They hope to reduce empty talk that does not contribute to the facts, so that everything done is practical work, and the greatest effect will be achieved in the final struggle.

The Greater America Evening News

Comments on Japan's Actions Towards China

They Are Truly Barbaric Means

They Are Truly the Means of a Mob

They Are Truly the Means of Brutal Beasts

The Greater America Evening News commented: "Our handling of cases, without weighing the circumstances or adhering to the law, acting rashly and imposing punishments directly, regardless of whether the punished is a genuine infringement or a perceived one, all constitute barbaric behavior. If a country resolves disputes with another country by acting as the plaintiff, judge, juror, and executor all in one, it poses a danger to the entire civilized world. This is the position Japan finds itself in today. It condones its military warlords, disregards its guarantees of peaceful arbitration, and brandishes its power against China. No one can doubt that Japan has many grievances against China, and other countries cannot be entirely unsympathetic to Japan's desire to resolve outstanding issues quickly. However, even with the most legitimate reasons, one cannot resort to erroneous actions. We witness Japan acting willfully, occupying Manchuria by force, bombing and shooting, using both guns and artillery, and seizing control of civil administration and the economy, while disregarding the instrument it had long signed with China, guaranteeing that both sides would abandon war as a means of resolving disputes. Our extreme disapproval of Japan is not about the fairness of its complaints against China, but about the imprudence and unfairness of the means it uses to resolve them. All civilized countries in the world prohibit individuals from retaliating against the suffering they have endured from their fellow human beings through violent means and instead first appeal to the state. Therefore, civilized countries also make solemn pledges that when disputes arise with other countries, they will propose peaceful arbitration before taking warlike action. Now, to insist that the occupation of Manchuria is limited to a corner of the region is both laughable and nonsensical. It must be understood that the stationing of Japanese troops on purely Chinese soil, which provokes Chinese suffering, cannot be confined to any one corner for long. Japan must also be aware of this. Once this kind of suffering and resentment erupts, it will be sufficient cause for war. Therefore, as an objective journalist, we maintain our position, as the principle of due legal process has already been recognized as the key to the happiness of the entire people of each country and as the key to civilization. Although the world sometimes fails to do so, only barbarians do not even follow it today, and only barbarians completely disregard it. Hasty retaliation is no longer tolerated in countries that pride themselves on civilization, just as it is not allowed among individuals in civilized countries. Therefore, we dare to assert that even if Japan's accusations against China are justified in three hundred cases, the means that Japan has used to seek justice are truly barbaric, truly the means of a mob, and truly the means of brutal beasts. They can only be implemented after the entire structure of civilization has been shattered."

After Kang Baosen's Suicide

The Proceeds from Selling His Clothes and Belongings

Are Entirely Used for the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Fund

Kang Baosen, a native of Liaoning Province, was 25 years old and served as a second lieutenant platoon leader in the sixth company of the second battalion of the third infantry regiment of the Ministry of Finance's Tax Police Corps. During the recent invasion of Chinese territory by violent Japan, as foreign aggression intensified, he felt that the country was being destroyed and the family was being ruined, and that it was better to die for the country than to live a meaningless life. Therefore, his usual remarks were exceptionally慷慨激昂, and he always wanted to fight a desperate battle with the Japanese, but he was limited by the current environment and could not fulfill his wish. Full of righteous indignation and unable to express his accumulated resentment, he suddenly took a Mauser pistol at 2 PM on the seventh of this month, when no one was paying attention, and fired a shot at his head. When the officers and soldiers of the company heard the sound and rushed over, he had already fallen to the ground, bleeding from his head, which was extremely tragic. The Songhu Garrison Headquarters immediately dispatched a car to send him to the Chinese Red Cross for help, but his injuries were severe, and he died at 5 PM that afternoon. He left behind three notes, one expressing his grief over the impending demise of the country and urging the people to strive for self-salvation, the second instructing people to sell his clothes and belongings after his death and use all the proceeds for the anti-Japanese national salvation fund, and the third providing the contact address of his family. After his death, all the officers and soldiers of the entire battalion were filled with resentment and shed tears, filled with righteous indignation, vowing to repay the country with sincere iron blood and loyalty to comfort the heroic soul of Martyr Kang. Commander Xiong has now issued 200 yuan for burial expenses, and Battalion Commander Han Buqing has dispatched Company Commander Mei Jie and several platoon leaders to collect the body and transport it to the Jilu Villa on Jinyi Road for temporary storage. The officers and soldiers of the regiment plan to hold a memorial service at the public sports field on the 12th.

Another

Committing Suicide Out of Grief and Indignation Over Violent Japan

Leaving Behind a Suicide Note After Jumping into the Huangpu River

Hoping that People Can Identify His Appearance and Clothing in Haste

At about 6 PM the night before last, the No. 1 ferry boat at the Xinkuan Wharf on Hankou Road

Page 14

was carrying about 20 passengers to the Chunjiang Wharf in Pudong. Unexpectedly, when the boat reached the center of the river, a middle-aged man suddenly jumped into the Huangpu River and committed suicide. The crew members tried desperately to rescue him, but he had already sunk to the bottom of the river and was forever with the river god. Only a newspaper, an anti-Japanese aggression alert, and a letter were left on the boat (with the address "No. 13, Xiangshun Lane, Baoshan Road, Zhabei, Zhao Yuncan, etc." written on it). The boat boss, Shen Heshang, was unable to rescue him and had no choice but to send the belongings to the water patrol station, explaining the circumstances of the deceased's jump into the river and saying that in the haste, he could not discern his appearance or clothing. The original text of his suicide note is copied below: "To the captain of the boat, I am truly sorry for committing suicide by jumping off your boat. Thank you. The reason for my suicide is purely because national difficulties are imminent, and I myself have no ability to save the country and am unworthy of being a citizen. After my death, please, sir, give me the merit of salvaging my body, and you will surely have high hopes in the future. Please." Upon reading it, the Chinese officers of the patrol station were all filled with regret. Even the Westerners recognized that he had acted out of patriotic impulse. The patrol station has now ordered investigators to investigate the deceased's family so that people can be sent to salvage the deceased's body.

Song Ziwen Convened Yesterday

Financial Stability Meeting

Decided that Various Government Bonds Would Be Purchased by Various Banks as Much as Possible; Restrictions on Spot Deliveries at the Exchange Would Be Lifted

Finance Minister Song Ziwen convened a meeting with the banking community in Shanghai yesterday at the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Finance. Representatives from 18 banks, including the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Central Bank, Yanye Bank, Jin Cheng Bank, Continental Bank, Zhongnan Bank, Shanghai Bank, China Industrial Bank, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Siming Bank, Zhongfu Bank, Tongshang Bank, Jiangsu Bank, Guohuo Bank, Kenye Bank, Xingye Bank, and Guohua Bank, attended. Finance Minister Song Ziwen chaired the meeting, reported on the purpose of convening the meeting, and the necessity of maintaining government bonds. After a long discussion by the representatives, they all agreed that maintaining the price of government bonds was the best way to stabilize the financial situation. Although the banks had previously released a loan of 15 million, there was still a surplus at present. However, when necessary, the banks should still lend as much as possible and purchase from the exchanges and banks as much as possible. On the other hand, the Ministry of Finance was requested to approve the cancellation of the restrictions on spot deliveries if the exchanges requested it, so that merchants could trade as much as possible. Song expressed his approval of this point. The meeting adjourned at 4:30 PM. A reporter from the Huadong News Agency specifically visited Vice Minister of Finance Zhang Shouyong regarding the Ministry of Finance's maintenance of government bonds. According to Zhang, the credit of various government bonds in China was originally very good, but the market situation fluctuated due to the Japanese taking the opportunity to cause trouble and merchants engaging in speculation. The Ministry of Finance had always paid great attention to maintaining government bonds. This meeting was an internal matter. It has now been decided that the banks will purchase as much as possible, and the market situation should stabilize. The peace negotiations between Nanjing and Guangdong have already yielded results. As for the Japanese warships coming to China, although their nature contains a demonstrative meaning, Shanghai is an international trading port, and Japan would never dare to risk the disapproval of the world and start a war lightly. He sincerely hopes that all merchants in Shanghai will remain calm, and the financial market can also be stable. As for the Ministry of Finance maintaining government bonds, it will always be responsible, no matter how bad the country gets.

The Municipal Party Department Orders Within Two Weeks

To Resolve Labor-Management Disputes

Labor and Management Unite to Overcome National Difficulties

Disputes Have Gradually Decreased

The Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department of the Chinese Kuomintang issued a notice to various trade associations and labor unions, stating that Japan is relying on its strength to invade China and commit aggression against our country. All Chinese people should unite and make every effort to fight against foreign aggression to save the country from danger. During this period, all industries and businesses in the city should be vigilant in their responsibilities to share the same boat and not engage in labor-management disputes that lead to infighting. Those that have already occurred must be resolved within two weeks of the date of the notice. As for those who intend to propose new conditions that have not been proposed, they should also be postponed to ensure that labor and management are united to overcome national difficulties. In addition to distributing and sending letters to the Social Affairs Bureau for reference, it is hereby urgently ordered that all industrial and commercial organizations in the city must comply with this order without fail. The industrial and commercial sectors in the city, in view of the national crisis, are reducing the already occurred labor-management disputes in order to seek unity against foreign aggression after receiving the notice from the Special Municipal Party Department and preparing to comply with the order and find ways to resolve them. For example, silk weaving workers, who originally proposed to improve treatment conditions, have now decided at the general meeting to postpone their proposals in order to unite labor and management to overcome national difficulties. According to the Municipal Party Department, labor-management disputes have decreased compared to before after violent Japan occupied the three northeastern provinces.

Please Accommodate the Guangdong Side's Request

Today, the party and the country are in extreme danger. Do you and the comrades know this? Only then can our party restore its credibility. At this time, the only key is for Mr. Hu to come to Shanghai. I deeply believe that Mr. Hu will be able to join hands with General Jiang to maintain the overall situation. I am willing to guarantee with my personality and life. In terms of personality and knowledge, only you and Mr. Hu. The Premier is the national father, and Mr. Hu is trusted by the national father. The classics say that what parents love, one should also love. You and I train young people with loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, and love every day, but we cannot do our best to restore Mr. Hu's freedom. We are truly ashamed. We have nothing to comfort the spirit of the Premier in heaven. When I was in Nanjing, I often visited Mr. Hu and talked with him wildly about old times in his youth, hoping to comfort him. Mr. Hu is extremely heartbroken, and some people still say that Mr. Hu does not want to leave Nanjing. Must Mr. Hu be depressed to the end? Otherwise, why would Mr. Hu say this? What has Mr. Hu done to harm the party and the country that he must be placed in this extreme situation? Is this how to assist Mr. Jiang and love Mr. Jiang? The decline of righteousness and the end of the party and the country. We have nothing to face the Premier. We are sinners of China. The people cannot forgive us. I have been engaged in the revolution since the end of the Qing Dynasty and have been struggling for more than twenty years. Although I served as an official in the Northern Court, I was actually working for the party. Comrades with a history in the party all know this and can say it. When I returned in my later years, the Premier loved and trusted me deeply. On his deathbed, he still murmured words of comfort. Seeing the country destroyed and the party ruined, I felt even more pain than any other comrade. Writing this, I do not know where my tears should come from. Your brother Zheng Hong's age.

Sailing on the Shanghai Maru

The American aviator Charles Lindbergh and his wife arrived in Shanghai from Wuhan and stayed for two nights. Later, due to the death of his father-in-law, they were eager to return home. They boarded the Japan Mail Steamship Company's Shanghai Maru at 9 AM yesterday morning to return home. Yesterday, more than 30 people, including the American consul and the directors of China Aviation Corporation, as well as their friends, went to the pier to see them off. Lindbergh and his wife boarded the ship at 7:40 AM. He expressed his deep regret for this. His wife's eyes were swollen like peaches from crying for days. It is said that when Lindbergh arrives in Nagasaki, he will take a train to Yokohama on the same day and then take the American mail ship Jackson President back to the United States. As for Lindbergh's plane left in Shanghai, it will be transported to the United States by China Aviation Corporation.

The Bureau of Social Affairs Pays Attention to Counterfeit National Products

Verification and Certification Starting From October 1st

Our country's production is backward, and foreign goods are rampant. It is impossible to revitalize the industry without supporting the products of domestic goods manufacturers. And merchants often use foreign goods to impersonate domestic brands in an attempt to make profits, which is especially hateful. Therefore, the Bureau of Social Affairs ordered the National Goods Exhibition Hall to prepare measures for the certification of domestic goods, conduct thorough investigations, and submit them for approval. Yesterday, the museum received instructions stating: "The submission has been received and the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce has been ordered to forward it to all trade associations for notification, and letters have been sent to the Public Security Bureau and newspapers for reference." The implementation plan for its certification is divided into: (1) Starting from October 1st of this year, the certification of domestic goods in the Shanghai urban area will be handled by the Shanghai National Goods Exhibition Hall. (2) All domestic goods manufacturers that have been certified by various agencies and organizations should immediately submit their certification documents to the National Goods Exhibition Hall for filing and verification and will be issued a certificate. (3) The newspapers will be informed that advertisements for all brands that have not been certified by the National Goods Exhibition Hall will not be allowed to use the words "National Goods" to prevent confusion.

Fire at Shangwen Road

Also, Three Children Missing

Unknown if They Perished in the Flames

Yesterday morning at 3:45 AM, a fire suddenly broke out in the upstairs residence of Wang Ligui, a Zhenjiang native who deals in imitation jadeite, located at No. 5 Renfuli, Shangwen Road, Nanshi. In an instant, the fire spread rapidly. Moreover, due to the strong easterly wind at the time, although fire trucks from the northwest and west districts of the Fire Brigade were dispatched to fight the fire, the effect was minimal, and it spread to the houses on the left and opposite, engulfing more than ten houses. It wasn't until 5:30 AM, nearly two hours later, that the fire was finally extinguished. Firefighter No. 68 from the North District Fire Brigade fell from the upper floor and suffered serious injuries. Director Xia from the West District also suffered minor injuries. Both were sent to the hospital by ambulance for treatment. At the time, the police chief of the Second Sub-Bureau of the two districts arrived at the scene to maintain order. Wang Ligui, the fire's originator, and Liu Weizhi, who lived downstairs, both fled in fear of being held responsible. Consequently, Wang's wife, Zhang, was taken to the sub-bureau. After a brief interrogation by the chief, she confessed to being 34 years old and from Zhenjiang, directly admitting that the fire had started, but the reason was that a fellow villager named Chang Jinzi had come from Zhenjiang to Shanghai and was staying at their place. It was probably that Yang carelessly threw a cigarette butt onto easily flammable, tattered cotton wadding, resulting in this misfortune. However, there are still three children missing, and it is unknown whether they perished in the flames. According to the chief's report, he immediately prepared a document to submit to the general bureau for verification.

Scavenging Woman Crushed to Death by Car

A young woman from Jiangbei, Zhou Xu, approximately in her thirties, made a living by scavenging. Yesterday morning around 7:00 AM, while scavenging in the Bund area outside Sima Road, a freight truck drove up from behind. The concession registration number was 17019. Because it was driving too fast, she was unable to avoid it in time and was knocked to the ground, suffering crushing injuries to her head, waist, and other areas, and her right foot was broken. She was on the verge of death. Subsequently, two Chinese constables, No. 940 and No. 214, from the Central Police Station arrived and impounded the truck at the police station for punishment. The injured person was immediately taken to Renji Hospital for treatment, but unfortunately, her injuries were too severe, and she died half an hour after arriving at the hospital. The body was then transferred by the hospital to the coroner's office for examination.

Shi Hongxun and Others Resign from City Federation Branch

Shi Hongxun, Wu Zifan, Qi Sheng, and others, executive committee members of the 23rd branch of the Shanghai Citizens' Federation, previously requested to resign from their positions on the 23rd executive committee of the Jin branch due to being overwhelmed with matters. The City Federation replied with a letter of retention, urging Shi and others to make an effort to continue. After the resignation of Shi and others, considering the current national crisis, they should have complied with the reply and returned to their posts. However, due to the concerns of their own businesses and being burdened with work, they truly had no spare time to serve as executive committee members of the branch. Rather than causing delays in the future, it would be better to resign first to give way to more capable individuals. Therefore, they sent another letter to the City Federation a few days ago, earnestly requesting permission to resign.

Life Weekly Publishes Special Issue on National Day and National Mourning

"Life Weekly," published by the Shanghai Hualong Road Life Weekly, has a pure purpose and fair opinions. It is published every Saturday and has never missed an issue for five years. It is learned that the issue to be published by the company on October 10, Volume 6, Issue 42, coincides with the Double Tenth Festival, and a special issue of "National Day and National Mourning" will be published. The volume will be approximately three times larger than the original. In addition to Tao Fen's "National Day and National Mourning," Chen Binhe's "The Northeast Problem in the Midst of National Crisis," Pan Yineng's "China in the Past Year," Hu Yuzhi's "International Affairs in the Past Year," Xinsheng's "World Trends and China's Future," Hansong's "The Problem of People," Baofu's "Scientific Life," Haofeng's "Lingering Shadows of a European Tour," a reporter's "Heartbreaking Sights," Chen Li's Japan Correspondence "Overseas Chinese in Japan after the Fall of Manchuria," "Rapid Developments after the Riot," and more than ten other sharp and insightful articles, there will also be eight pages of Double Tenth Pictorials exquisitely printed by Ge Gongzhen using phototype printing, which are both interesting and valuable. The price remains the same as before, with a yearly subscription fee of one dollar and fifty cents domestically and four dollars internationally. Major bookstores in various ports sell it.

The long-awaited new film "Red Tears Shadow" has been scheduled to premiere today simultaneously in nine major theaters in Shanghai, including Central, New Central, and Star, as well as in Hangzhou, Suzhou, Wuxi, Nanjing, and other foreign ports. This film is the Star Film Company's greatest production of the year, a successful masterpiece directed by Zheng Zhengqiu. It took a year to produce and cost a huge sum of one hundred thousand yuan. Its excellent results are sufficient to rival Western films. The main actors, Hu Die, Zheng Xiaoqiu, and Xia Peizhen, perform earnestly and are all well-suited to their characters. All the sets and costumes were specially designed and produced by assistant director Cai Chusheng, and they are beautiful and pleasing to the eye, unprecedented. The overall layout and structure of the film are tortuous and novel, and the photography and lighting are clear. Everything contains beauty. It is expected that after the premiere, it will receive a warm welcome from the audience.

Zhabei Xing Cai Market Begins Construction

Yang De , Dai Yushan, Zhu Yiqin, and other gentry merchants of Zhabei, considering that the vegetable stalls along Gonghe Xin Road and Datong Road are dense, obstructing traffic, and endangering sanitation, initiated the construction of a two-story steel-reinforced concrete vegetable market and twenty-six city buildings at the intersection of Datong Road and Zhongxing Road. They have successively received Housing License No. 1625 and Vegetable Market License No. 1721 issued by the Public Works Bureau. The wood and materials have all been procured, and all construction work is contracted by Yang Deji Construction Factory. Local News Two

Disaster Relief News

Suzhou Flood Relief Association and Others

Request Allocation of Six Million in Disaster Relief Public Bonds

The association recently sent a telegram to the Central Disaster Relief Committee, along with the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association, the Jiangsu Provincial Disaster Relief Association, and the Jiangbei Flood Relief Temporary Relief Association, requesting the allocation of six million yuan in disaster relief public bonds for relief. The original telegram is recorded below: "To the Shanghai National Government Disaster Relief Committee, we respectfully report that this year's flood in Jiangsu Province has affected fifty counties. The number of disaster victims is nearly ten million, the area is vast, and the situation is truly unprecedented in a century. We have repeatedly telegraphed appeals, and we trust that this has reached your attention. However, in the past two months, official relief and charitable relief have raised at most one million yuan in total from all sources. When distributed to various counties, even those with more funds received only thirty to forty thousand yuan. We have repeatedly received requests for relief from various areas, stating that the funds previously allocated only benefit each disaster victim with a few jiao, and those counties awaiting relief continue to send telegrams requesting assistance. Unfortunately, the relief funds raised by our association and others have already been fully allocated, and there is nothing left to respond with. Moreover, the number of people coming and going to various shelters has been no less than several hundred thousand. Among them, the elderly and weak who are helpless, unable to advance and unable to retreat, still number more than forty thousand as of now. Each person in the shelter needs one jiao worth of food per day, and each shelter is expected to operate for four months, which requires no less than five to six hundred thousand yuan. In addition, there are still the majority of disaster victims in the disaster areas who are desperately clinging to their homes, hoping that after the flood recedes, they can engage in winter farming. However, it is expected that it will be difficult for the accumulated water to recede completely in the shortest period. When the cold wind rises, they will have neither clothing nor food, and those in the countryside will inevitably flock to the shelters, competing for supplies. The number of people will be ten times greater than today, crying from hunger and cold, a truly pitiful situation. We cannot bear to drive them away, nor can we support them for a long time. Therefore, we must make preparations for lending seeds, pledging cattle, repairing houses, and providing clothing. Sitting and watching all these things, we cannot come up with a plan. Therefore, on the first day of this month, our association and others convened a joint meeting, discussed in detail, and proposed to resubmit the case of requesting the issuance of six million yuan in disaster relief public bonds, based on the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association's telegram of the previous month, in the name of the joint meeting. This is truly because we recognize the severity of the disaster in Jiangsu Province and the eagerness with which various places await relief. If there are no large amounts of funds for assistance, all the disaster victims will inevitably face the prospect of starting to live and ending up dying. Therefore, we once again jointly send a telegram to earnestly request that you examine the previous case and approve the allocation of six million yuan from the disaster relief public bond funds, so as to thoroughly relieve the disaster, broadly prepare for the aftermath, and assist the Central Government's supreme intention of universal love and benevolence. This is our most sincere prayer. We await your command, and we eagerly anticipate your reply."

Canal Project Association

Suggestion to Establish a Deliberative Council Quickly

The Disaster Relief Association stationed in Zhen, Yancheng, Taizhou, and Dongtai, which is concerned about the breach in the canal embankment, has repeatedly expressed its views. Now, it is sending a telegram to the Canal Project Rehabilitation Committee, requesting that it convene a deliberative council quickly and amend the committee's organizational outline. The original text is recorded as follows: "To the Jiangsu Jiangbei Canal Project Rehabilitation Committee, the canal embankment has been breached for forty days, and your committee has been established for nearly a month. There is still no date for the closure of the breach and the interruption of the flow. How the various sections of the project will be rehabilitated, we have not heard anything about it. We have repeatedly received telegrams from various counties inquiring about the situation, and it is difficult to answer. We believe that your committee's previous resolution to establish a deliberative council was also because it recognized that it is inappropriate to be deeply closed and firmly rejected. It is better to be open and fair to gain wider hearing. We deeply rejoice in this. We propose that you convene the meeting quickly to dispel doubts and comfort public opinion. However, the original organizational outline regarding the deliberative council's powers only allows it to accept project reports and review income and expenditure. These are all ex post facto recognitions, and it does not grant the power to agree to the engineering plan beforehand. It seems that it has not yet reached perfection. Whether it should be revised further, we propose that you rule on it together. Disaster Relief Association stationed in Zhen, Yancheng, Taizhou, and Dongtai. "

Report of the Disaster Relief Medical Team

The medical team for treating disaster victims organized by the Shanghai National Medicine Association is working in the shelters every day and has achieved good results. The following is an excerpt from the treatment statistics for the most recent half month: Dysentery 592 people, typhoid fever 322 people, common cold 190 people, swelling 224 people, chest congestion, 55 people, summer heat 4 people, cold fever 4 people, vomiting and diarrhea 14 people, malnutrition 12 people, dropsy 1 person, sores and infections 64 people, injuries from falls 2 people, wind disease 10 people, malaria 98 people, food stagnation 99 people, consumption 25 people, postpartum 60 people, seasonal sha 4 people, depression 3 people, athlete's foot X people, bloody stools 15 people, hernia 5 people, ophthalmology 24 people, measles 31 people, headache 4 people, amenorrhea 3 people, hemoptysis 3 people, backache 1 person, dental disease 7 people, nasal bleeding 3 people, chancre 2 people, vomiting ascarids 13 people, defecating ascarids 2 people, asthma 20 people, rectal prolapse 1 person, jaundice 9 people, epilepsy 1 person, phlegm retention 13 people, total 1939 people. Bao Long Hospital

Whether Negligence of Duty

The Circumstances of the Death of Cheng Xiechun's Eldest Son

A Letter Requesting Public Judgment from Various Important Organizations

Cheng Xiechun, the owner of the Shanghai Xie Ji Bookstore, sent letters to various important organizations in Shanghai yesterday, stating: "I respectfully report that my eldest son, Jingan, was hospitalized and treated at Bao Long Hospital on Baker Road, Shanghai, due to illness, but he died due to negligence. The circumstances are as follows: On September 18 of this year, I accompanied him into the hospital. According to the hospital doctor's diagnosis, it was tuberculous peritonitis and pneumonia. He was X-rayed once and sunlamped twice. During the second sunlamp treatment, the person in charge of the sunlamp left the patient under the sunlamp to have lunch. The patient waited for a long time and did not return. Due to excessive heat, he could no longer bear it and had to forcibly rise from the bed and turn off the sunlamp himself. On September 28, the hospital performed surgery on the patient without seeking my consent or signature. The anesthesia was incomplete, causing the patient to scream, struggle, and bleed profusely, and his spirit suddenly declined. After the operation, no doctor or nurse from the hospital attended to the patient or prepared for immediate remedy, causing the patient to die unfortunately. I am writing to request a public judgment on whether this kind of action by the hospital constitutes negligence of duty and leads to death. I would be very grateful if you would uphold justice."

Three Days After the Wedding

Only to Find Out She Was Someone's Concubine

The Seventeen-Year-Old Bride Could Only Sob

Yu Qiusheng Insisted That What's Done is Done

Both Parties Have Now Filed Lawsuits Separately

The Location of the Marriage Still Needs Investigation

Yu Qiusheng, the owner of the Dade Rubber Factory, is over forty years old and has been married for many years. This summer, he suddenly had the absurd idea of taking a concubine. However, taking a concubine is not only not allowed by law, but a girl from a good family is even more unwilling to commit herself to such matters. Therefore, he falsely claimed that his wife had died and, for the sake of descendants, held a second wedding, asking people to search everywhere for a beautiful woman to fill the lower ranks. Thus, a woman from Shaoxing named Wang, who lived in Xinkang Lane, Datong Road, Xinzha, was fooled by matchmakers and agreed to marry her seventeen-year-old daughter to Yu. The wedding was set for July 23. The groom's residence specially rented the New World Hotel as the wedding hall, while the bride's residence rented the Hongxiang Hotel as the departure point. When the auspicious day arrived, Yu used a procession of a hundred cars decorated with ribbons to welcome the bride, and he asked Ms. Wang Linzhu and Ms. Wang Qiaoxian to accompany the bride. Although there was no drum music, the red candles burned high, and they replaced the traditional bowing with mutual bows. After the ceremony, they feasted and entertained guests, and the bridal chamber was at No. 9 Tongde Lane, Zilai Street, French Concession. Three days later, Yu said to the bride, "Now, there are relatives who have prepared a banquet, would you like to come with me?" The bride did not know what it was for and happily went with him. At No. 66 Zhangchuan Lane in the city, she met a middle-aged woman whom Yu introduced as his sister, ordering the bride to address her as "Sister." After the banquet, the bride wanted to go home, but Yu and the middle-aged woman both stopped her. Soon, all the appliances in the Tongde Lane bridal chamber were completely moved to the middle-aged woman's house, and a separate room was prepared for the bride. Seeing this situation, the bride felt as if she had fallen into a fog. At night, the bride was alone in the deep boudoir, waiting for Yu to arrive. When she asked others, they all said that he was sleeping with his sister. Only then did she realize that what he called his sister was actually a disguised term for his wife. The bride knew this trickery, but with no relatives to rely on, she could only sob and cry. Yu and his wife were afraid that the bride would run away at night, and they watched her very closely, not allowing her to take a step beyond the boundary. When the honeymoon arrived, the bride's mother went to visit her beloved daughter. When they met, the daughter told her everything. The mother immediately took her daughter to the Dade Rubber Factory's office and accused Yu of not cheating on the marriage. Yu, having achieved his goal, said to his mother-in-law, "What's done is done now. It's useless to argue. You should advise your daughter to be content with her life." Hearing his words, Wang felt that Yu was too deceitful and could not tolerate it. Therefore, on the 26th of last month, she took her daughter and hired a lawyer to send a letter to the Public Concession Police Station, requesting to report him according to law to uphold ethics. Wang Yaotang, the police station's lawyer, then filed a public prosecution against Yu Qiusheng for bigamy based on Article 254 of the Criminal Law. While this was in progress, Yu also hired a lawyer to accuse Wang's daughter of running away with money to the French Concession Police Station. The case was once tried by the Second Special District Court of the French Concession and adjourned to be heard again on the 14th of this month. Yesterday morning, Feng Shide, a judge of the Criminal Court of the First Special District Court of the Public Concession, opened the court to hear the bigamy case filed by the police station. First, the police station's lawyer stated the circumstances of the case. The defendant's lawyer argued that this case should also be transferred to the French Concession for joint trial, while the plaintiff's lawyer expressed opposition. Then, the bride testified about the location of the marriage, saying that she only lived in the French Concession for three days after the marriage before moving to the city. The police station also summoned Zhou Shunjin, an employee of the New World Hotel, to the stand to prove the circumstances of the marriage. However, Zhou's testimony was quite evasive. The defendant also insisted that he only held a banquet at the hotel and did not formally marry. Finally, Judge Feng stated that the jurisdiction of this case should be determined by the location of the marriage. Where the marriage was actually held still needs to be investigated. Therefore, this issue cannot be resolved yet. The defendant was ordered to pay a security deposit of two thousand yuan, and the hearing was adjourned to the 15th of this month after the investigation is clear.

Incense Burning and Candle Lighting at Xia Hai Temple

Bandits Prayed for Divine Protection

Hoping to Kill Two People and Rob Their Clothes and Ornaments

Hoping the Case Would Never Be Solved

Ma Er Had Torn Clothes as Evidence

Heaven's Net is Vast, But Nothing Escapes Its Mesh

Late at night on the 19th of last month, Gu Cao, the aunt-in-law of Zhu Yangshan, and Zhou Lu, a maidservant, at the home of Zhu Yangshan above the Yichang Electrical Company at 196 Dong Xi Hua De Road, were suddenly murdered by bandits, and clothes and ornaments worth 1,038 yuan were robbed. Cai Zhitian, a Chinese detective of the Huishan Police Station, arrested Ma Er, a suspect from Tongzhou, and handed him over to the First Special District Court for interrogation. He denied the charges and was detained for investigation. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen Bingrong sat in the Third Criminal Court to continue the hearing. The police station's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, stated that during the adjournment, the defendant confessed the details to the police station. The defendant in this case was the driver of Cai Detective. Previously, Cai Detective searched for a white cloth shirt abandoned by the murderer at the scene of the murder of the victims Gu and Zhou. It had blood stains on it, and the pocket on the shirt was patched. Cai Detective carefully examined the pocket of the white cloth shirt worn by the driver Ma Er on a daily basis, and it also had traces of patching, with similar dimensions and length. When asked about it, he took out the same shirt for inspection and vehemently denied it. However, Ma was highly suspected in this case, so he was brought to trial. Later, a fellow worker proved that the bloody shirt was indeed Ma Er's, and there was another slight tear at the button. It was what he used to wear in the past. Therefore, Cai Detective and the Western detective re-interrogated him at the police station, and he finally confessed that the case was initiated by a certain A and other three fugitives. They knew that the victim's family had a savings of 500 yuan in cash and that only two women were taking care of the house, making it easier to plan. Therefore, on the evening of the 17th of this month, at around 9:00 PM, they had a meal at a small restaurant near Longqing Lane and spent two yuan discussing it. They decided to carry it out and went to Xia Hai Temple in Yangshupu to burn incense and light candles, praying for divine protection to prevent the case from being solved. If they were arrested, they would not betray their accomplices and would rather be sacrificed alone, swearing solemn oaths. That night, they went to the restaurant again for a big meal and drank heavily. At around 1:00 AM, armed with knives and flashlights, they entered through the rear door of the house by climbing over the wall from a dark place. First, A pried open the door and they entered together. The defendant broke into the bedroom of the maidservant Zhou Lu, and she woke up and shouted for a robber. The defendant, in desperation, stabbed Zhou's head, abdomen, and other parts with a knife, killing her instantly. Blood gushed out like a spring. The defendant picked up old cloth nearby and covered it with it. A and others entered Gu Cao's room, trying to take out the 500 yuan in banknotes, but they failed and were also stabbed to death with knives. The maidservant Zhou Lu was only wearing a short shirt at the time and had no pants. Whether she was raped by these people beforehand is unknown. Afterwards, the defendant's accomplices grabbed clothes and ornaments and escaped. In the morning, they went to a pawnshop on Zhaofeng Road and pawned them, etc. The defendant received five yuan the first time and fifty yuan the second time. The defendant's confession, the shirt found in the broken cloth in the house, and a knife were presented for inspection and requested to be postponed. Ma Er firmly denied that the shirt belonged to him and said that the confession at the police station was not voluntary and was made up. He asked the court to be lenient and repeatedly cried out for injustice. After Judge Shen verified the confession, he ordered him to be returned to custody and adjourned the hearing for another day.

Inspection of Factories in the Concession

If a Formal Inspection is Desired

It Must Be Discussed with the Municipal Council

The Shanghai Evening Post & Mercury reported that after the factory inspectors of the Bureau of Social Affairs inspected factories in the International Settlement, the Western-organized Employers' Federation sent a letter to the Municipal Council with inquiries. Mr. Wu Shouchi’s News (Written For. Side. Hear. Propaganda.)

Upon hearing that the Japanese had forcibly occupied our Northeast, all people in the country were filled with righteous indignation, beating their chests and drinking blood. In particular, the ardent and fervent young students have organized petition groups, volunteer corps, and propaganda and lecture teams. For a time, the spirit of saving the country was truly admirable. One day, while I was returning from visiting a friend, I happened to see a propaganda team of students from a certain school lecturing to a rural villager. The lecturer was a handsome young man, dressed in a beautiful Western suit, his hair slicked back and shiny. When he spoke, all the villagers listened attentively. One listener, holding a hoe, with a bare, dark body, seemed to have come straight from the fields after work, deep in thought. After the student finished his speech, the villager said with emotion, "Since Japan has occupied our country, the only method for us Chinese people is to boycott Japanese goods. But you students can only talk but not act. Look at the clothes you are wearing now, aren't they Japanese goods? You propagandists buy Japanese goods and use Japanese goods, yet you dare to preach to others not to buy or use them? We ourselves wear homespun cloth and use homemade goods. We don't need you to tell us not to buy Japanese goods. We have never bought them. Those who are afraid to buy, it's still you, you better start by advertising to yourselves!” His words were impassioned, causing the propagandists of the team to blush and say nothing, turning away and leaving. Admirable, indeed, is this rural villager. Sent from Wusong, please publish in your esteemed newspaper.

(Reply) No matter what, if you advise others to do something, you must first do it yourself; if you advise others not to do something, you must first do it yourself. For the past two or thirty years, there have been too many people who speak nice words, but few who actually do, and even fewer who are willing to do it themselves first. The fact you reported can very well serve as a warning to people in all aspects, causing everyone to pay attention, not just to the matter of advocating not using Japanese goods.

Mr. Ma Yuliang’s News (Asking. About. People's. Work. Against. Japan.)

Currently, besides not using Japanese goods, advising the public not to use Japanese goods, joining the National Salvation Volunteer Corps, and propagating the brutal Japanese theft of our Eastern Provinces, what other things should our citizens be responsible for? Please, in your compassionate wisdom, publish an answer in the newspaper to comfort my patriotic heart.

(Reply) As a member of the Lishui business community, if you earnestly do the few things mentioned in your letter, I am afraid that you will already have done a lot of work and had a lot of influence. Speaking of things beyond that, there is one fundamental thing, which is that everyone must work harder in their respective positions. Officials, whether high or low, civil or military, should of course intensify their work. Even we ordinary people, farmers and workers, working harder can lead to a special increase in production; merchants working harder can lead to a double circulation of goods; students working harder in their studies can quickly improve their academic abilities; even we journalists are intensifying our work. If all the people in the country work harder together, production will especially increase, scientific research will be particularly advanced, and the operation of institutions will be particularly smooth. Everyone is willing to devote double the energy to fulfill their responsibilities. This is the foundation of a wealthy and strong country. I hope you will work hard, and we will all work hard.

Announcement Regarding Stamps

Affix this stamp when mailing correspondence

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the atmospheric pressure over the entire Asian continent is increasing rapidly. The weather here on the coast is cloudy and cold, with a good chance of rain. There are strong northeasterly winds over the Yellow Sea and the East China Sea. The weather is severe between the Ryukyu Islands and the Ogasawara Islands. The center of the winds was estimated at around 2:00 PM to be within 120 miles of 25 degrees north latitude and 135 degrees east longitude, moving northeast, and within 120 miles of 17 degrees north latitude and 137 degrees east longitude, moving northwest by north. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 79.2 degrees and the lowest was 66.9 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 80.6 degrees and the lowest was 54.5 degrees.
